Bian Jinlang (age 17, from Shasha), the younger brother of Bian Shunbao, the owner of Zhaojiji Tailor Shop in Ruifeng Silk Factory, No. 5 Workshop, No. 5 Jian Tou, outside the West Gate of the county, has been in Wuxi for many years and has been learning to be

Worker's Bone Crushed in Yarn Factory 108

At the Zhenxin Yarn Factory outside the West Gate, a male worker, Xu Wenying, in the yarn-spinning room, at approximately 1 PM yesterday, was working when, due to carelessness, his right hand was caught in a leather belt. He was thrown down from a height, crushing his arm bone. He immediately lost consciousness and was sent to Liu Jichuan's clinic of traumatology outside the West Gate for treatment. Although his life is not in danger, he is likely to be permanently disabled, which is truly tragic.

Changzhou 109

Kidnapping Case Occurs in the Third District 110

At He Pangeng's home in Qianjia Village, Wenyong Township, in the third district of Wuyi, over ten bandits suddenly arrived on the night of the 20th, each carrying a weapon. They kidnapped his seven-year-old son, Chunren, and looted all valuables and miscellaneous items in the house. Afterwards, the township head, Wang Zemin, reported the case to the county on the 22nd, requesting the dispatch of police to assist in the arrest and rescue the hostage.

Jiangyin 111

County Magistrate Li Investigates Private Settlement of Opium Offense 112

Since taking office, Chen Dun, the Chief of the Public Security Bureau, has strictly prohibited opium and gambling. On the 19th, he ordered Inspector Wang Wenzhong and employee Chen Fusheng to lead police to Huang Wantong's opium den outside the North Gate. They arrested Huang Zuyin, the owner of the small opium den, and seized opium paraphernalia at the home of Dr. Jiang Benli near Tongxing Lane. Subsequently, a member of the Chamber of Commerce interceded, and Huang Zuyin paid 300 yuan, while Jiang Benli paid 100 yuan to settle the case. On the 22nd, County Magistrate Li learned of this and immediately ordered legal police officer Liu Xiangting to arrest both Huang and Jiang outside the North Gate. While they were resting in the Chamber of Commerce, some people wanted to find a way to ease the situation to avoid complications, but County Magistrate Li refused. In the evening, both Huang and Jiang were taken to the county government, where Judge Wu Cheng interrogated them behind closed doors in an inner room for a long time before ordering them to leave. Judge Wu Cheng then went to Yiyuan to attend a banquet held by the Relief Institute for County Magistrate Li. At the county government gate, he asked Huang and Jiang, "Did you disclose anything you confessed just now to anyone outside?" They replied that they had not. Wu said, "If there is any leakage, you will be responsible." It is unknown what the final outcome will be.

Zhenjiang 113

Three Counter-Revolutionary Criminals Executed by Firing Squad 114

The Zhenjiang Provincial Government Military Law Tribunal interrogated counter-revolutionary criminals this Wednesday and sentenced Wang Jizhi, Lu Shiyuan, and Tan Zhizhong, all from Taixian, to death. Yesterday morning (the 23rd), they were taken from prison, bound to the execution ground, and executed by firing squad.

Patrol Chief Extortion Case Adjudicated 115

Liu Kebi, a patrol chief of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau's bicycle team, led police officers to inspect the station on March 27th and extorted money from opium offenders. The matter was discovered by the chief, who sent personnel to investigate and transferred the case to the court for investigation. Yesterday, he was sentenced to six months imprisonment and fined sixty yuan.

Arrest of Counterfeit Money User 116

Zhou Zhuohe from Hunan has recently been using counterfeit ten-yuan banknotes from a certain bank to purchase goods and receive change in silver dollars in Zhenjiang. Yesterday, Huaxin Shoe Store detected the counterfeit and reported it to the police, who arrested him. Several counterfeit banknotes were found on his person. Upon hearing the news, various defrauded businesses went to identify the suspect and reported to the Public Security Bureau. The bureau transferred Zhou to the court. Zhou's testimony was evasive, and he insisted that he borrowed the banknotes from a friend and did not know they were counterfeit. The court has dispatched officers to investigate the details with each defrauded business to determine the verdict.

Yangzhou 117

Bandit Zhuang Shiying Sentenced to Execution by Firing Squad 118

Zhuang Shiying, a notorious bandit from Siyang, previously apprehended by the Second District of the Water Police and handed over to the Governor's Office, has now been found guilty by the military court. Zhuang Shiying kidnapped Zhu Zhujie in Yugou, coerced her into marriage, and conspired with bandit leader Liu Guanzhi and others in Yugou, Keshu, and five other locations, to commit robbery and demand ransoms. He was sentenced to death in accordance with the regulations for punishing bandits. On the morning of the 22nd, Zhuang Shiying was bound and taken to the automobile road outside the Dayun Gate and executed by firing squad.

Rugao 119

Three Bandits Captured in Home Robbery Case 120

At the home of the Hu Ma family in the Jiangjiayuan area of Baitu Township, at about 10 PM the night before last, several bandits suddenly arrived, broke down the door, and tied up Mrs. Hu and her daughter with ropes and lead wire. They ransacked the house, stealing fifteen pieces of coarse cloth, numerous gold and silver ornaments, and thirty-nine silver dollars. Mrs. Hu sustained head injuries. The suspects in the case, Liu Ru, Zhou Songyan, and Cun Hou (also known as Yan Chen), have been arrested by Wu Minchu, the leader of the third detachment of the local defense corps stationed in the area. They were handed over to the county government for prosecution yesterday.

Nantong 121

Anti-Smuggling Bureau Forms Mobile Patrol Team 122

The Salt Affairs Anti-Smuggling Bureau of the Five Prefectures of Jiangsu, due to rampant salt smuggling and sluggish official sales in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River and along the coast, has specially appointed Chen Xisun to form the Jianghai Mobile Patrol Team in Chongming, dedicated to mobile patrols.

Sands and Reed Fields of Shazhou Subject to Tax and Grain Supplement 123

The Liu Hai Shazhou reed fields of Nantong have been inspected by the Finance Department and found to be mostly mature. The county government and finance bureau have been ordered to assess taxes and supplement grain accordingly. If there are any collapses along the river, they should be investigated and reported for exemption.

Ferry Capsizes at Hekou Town 124

At the ferry crossing in Tangzha Hekou Town, Nantong, a ferry capsized on the morning of the 22nd due to excessive loading, resulting in over twenty deaths.

Pinghu 125

Impoverished Woman Attempts Suicide Due to Husband's Illness 126

Ye Xinglin, a native of Ningbo residing in Xincang Town, made a living selling eggs. Recently, due to slow business and financial difficulties, he became ill from worry and resentment and was bedridden. Yesterday morning, Ye's wife, seeing her husband critically ill and fearing he could not be saved, conceived a desire to end her life. Taking advantage of a moment when no one was watching, she took poison and attempted suicide. The family discovered her and immediately called a doctor to treat her. She had been poisoned deeply and her life is in danger.

Pessimistic Outlook for Silkworm Season in Eastern Townships 127

In the eastern townships of this county, the weather turned suddenly cold after the third sleep of the silkworms during this silkworm season, coupled with continuous rain. The silkworms consumed wet leaves and died, spitting yellow water after the major sleep. Therefore, a positive outcome for this silkworm season is unlikely.

Jiaxing 128

Puyuan Town Looted by Bandits 129

In Puyuan Town, at the border of Jiaxing and Tongxiang, around 5 AM on the 23rd, dozens of bandit ships suddenly arrived with over a hundred bandits, all armed with guns. They swarmed ashore, first looting the firearms of the stationed water police, the Jiaxing-Tongxiang Public Security Bureau branches, and the local defense corps. After killing one police officer from the Public Security Bureau, they began looting various businesses separately. None of the medium-sized or larger businesses were spared. Around 8 AM, they began to loot and escaped towards Xincheng. By the time the military and police officials in Hecheng received the news, they immediately telegraphed the commander of the Third District Water Police and the mobile patrol team stationed in Zhouquan to block all the main roads, but the bandits had already fled far away. It is reported that the Gongyi Pawnshop suffered the greatest losses among the looted businesses, while gold shops and cloth stores also suffered substantial losses.

Hospital Director Narrowly Escapes Kidnapping by Bandits 130

Xia Zhenwen, the director of Jiaxing Hospital, was invited to see a patient at No. 16 Xieqiao Street in the south of the city the day before yesterday. However, upon arriving, there was no patient there, only a woman and two young men. After Dr. Xia went upstairs, the two young men demanded a loan of two thousand yuan from Xia. When Xia said he had no money, he was threatened in various ways. Fortunately, Xia was resourceful and managed to escape. The next day, Dr. Xia received a threatening letter instructing him to prepare the money and send it. After the County Public Security Bureau learned of this, they dispatched a wooden-cased gun team to search the house at No. 16 Xieqiao Street. They found a woman living there, but the two young men were nowhere to be found. The county bureau has now learned the names of the two young men and is conducting a strict investigation.

Ningbo 131

Zheng Yunkun's Son Kidnapped 132

Zheng Yunkun, a merchant in Longshan Ximen, north of the town, was quite wealthy. Zheng has now passed away. His son, Xianxing, is only thirteen years old. However, at approximately 3 PM yesterday (the 21st), six bandits suddenly arrived, each carrying a handgun, and kidnapped Xianxing.

Starting Point: Corner of Carter Road and Jing'an Temple Road

丨Sixty-Eight People Set Off at 8:15 AM丨

Defeats Hujiang 28-23

丨Tonight at 8 PM vs. St. John's… Tomorrow vs. White Team丨The Black and White basketball team, which shook Pingjin, is campaigning in Shanghai. Tang Baokun's Prowess Not Diminished 136

Tang Baokun, one of the Five Tigers of Nankai, is agile and lively, known for his quickness and accurate shooting. This time, he came south as the mainstay of the Black and White team, working hard in offense and defense, directing advances and retreats. His agile figure and the prowess of a famous general have not diminished in the slightest, making him the most popular player. Left forward Shen Yugong cooperated very well with Tang.

Black and White Team Full of Promise 137

The Black and White team is a rising force in Tianjin. Last night, their individual skills were excellent. Their dribbling posture was beautiful and unmatched. Their shooting skills are not yet the most refined, and there were occasional mistakes, making them slightly inferior to the Northeast University team. Wang Xiliang commanded the entire team, performing meritorious and arduous service. Having been separated from Tang Baokun for a long time, facing him in a different army, he must have felt a sense of change.

Tianjin Team Displays Might in the Backcourt 139

The first half ended with Hujiang winning by three points. In the second half, Hujiang collapsed, and Black and White won 28-23.

Three National Records for Soochow Women's Track and Field 144

(1) High Jump (2) Long Jump (3) 50 Meters… Broken by Zhuang Mingzhen of Chenglie School

Yesterday's Results: Soochow Girls' Middle School First in Group A, Yinhua First in Group B

The second track and field meet of the Soochow Women's Athletic Association was held yesterday morning. The results were excellent, with Soochow Girls' Middle School winning the Group A team title, and Zhuang Mingzhen of Chenglie School breaking three national records in the high jump, long jump, and 50 meters. Details are as follows:

Heroines 145

Soochow society was initially quite rich in feudal forces, and active children were often scolded by their elders. As a result, progress in men's sports has been recent, let alone for women. This conference, because of the promotion and publicity, suddenly increased thousands of moving shadows and traces of footsteps among the fields of Zhujiazhuang, Changmen, creating an unprecedented event. The venue was set up at the Chenglie School's sports field, with Qingbai flags flying. A banner reading "Heroines" was hung high in front of the stage, and the audience suspected that all the Soochow ladies participating were female heroes like Hua Mulan.

Opening Ceremony 146

The opening ceremony was held at 9 AM. After performing the ceremony, the president, Lin Yunsheng, reported on the preparations, and Chen Zhenbang of the county party committee and You Yuefeng, the representative of the education bureau, gave speeches. Their words generally elaborated on sportsmanship and not forgetting the original curriculum. Then, the competition began. When more than eighty athletes paraded around the field with flags, and more than a hundred white legs walked along, it made some old men frown in surprise, but we thought it was beautiful.

Soochow Eccentric 147

丨Ms. Zhuang Zhen丨 148

More than eighty people participated in this competition. The track events adopted a semi-final system. Zhuang Mingzhen of Chenglie School usually ran the 50 meters in seven seconds, jumped one meter and thirty-five centimeters in the high jump, and four meters and fifty-five centimeters in the long jump. Sun Guiyun and Wu Meixian from Guandong are not her opponents. Is this not one of the eccentrics in Soochow's sports scene? Although Soochow Girls' Middle School has many talents, none can hope to match her.

Scores of Each School 149

After the competition was completed, Zhu Song and Sun concluded the results. The team title for Group A belonged to Soochow Girls' Middle School, and the team title for Group B belonged to Yinhua. Soochow Girls' Middle School scored 23 points, Chenglie 20 points, Jinghai 13 points, and Leyi 6 points in Group A. Yinhua scored 32 points, Jinghai 19 points, Leyi 10 points, and the women's vocational school 3 points in Group B. For individual total scores, Zhuang Mingzhen was first with 20 points, Zhu Shunying and Zhang Rongchu were second with 6 points each, and Zhang Yingfen was fourth with 5 points in Group A. Zou Shande was first with 13 points, Wu Jingzhen was second with 11 points, Gao Peizhen was third with 10 points, and Xue Guan was fourth with 8 points in Group B.

Closing Ceremony and Awards 150

The meeting ended after dark. Lin Yunsheng presented the awards. The prizes included Qian Tianpeng, Director of the Construction Bureau, a "Rising Step by Step" easel, Zou Jingzhi, Chief of the Public Security Bureau, a victory flag, a silver shield from Cuiying Middle School Patriotic Girls' School, and a silver cup from the Da Guangming Newspaper, etc. The winners laughed and held their prizes in the dim night, going their separate ways.

Brief History of Zhuang Mingzhen, Who Broke Three National Records 151

Zhuang Mingzhen, a student from Chenglie School who broke the national records in the long jump, high jump, and 50-meter race, is from Nanxiang and is 19 years old. She initially studied at Baoshan Normal School and entered Chenglie Physical Education School in Soochow this semester. She has a tall stature and does not have a girlish appearance. In the 50-meter preliminary, her stride was more than six feet, and her score was only seven seconds. Compared to the final, because she participated in too many events, her score was slightly inferior. According to the previous national record, the high jump was one meter and twenty-two centimeters, the long jump was four meters, and the 50-meter race was seven seconds and four tenths of a second, which has now been easily broken by Ms. Zhuang, speaking for the Soochow ladies, a good phenomenon in the sports world. If she can be trained further, Soochow women's sports will not be difficult to show their strength in the National Games and win championships. Ms. Zhuang, strive!

Five New Records 164

丨100 Meters丨200 Meters丨800 Meters丨1500 Meters丨Discus Throw丨

All five items are new meet records

Lin Guangxing emerges as a dark horse

In the two-day competition, a total of five new meet records were set: (1) Lin Guangxing of Shanghai University in the 100 meters with 11.1 seconds, breaking Huang Zhiming's 11.6 seconds; (2) Lin Guangxing of Shanghai University in the 200 meters with 23.2 seconds, breaking Zhou Xingjue's 24.4 seconds; (3) Meng Guangshun of Jinling University in the 800 meters with 2 minutes and 19 seconds, breaking Ma Shunwei's 2 minutes and 22 seconds; (4) Meng Guangshun of Jinling University in the 1500 meters with 4 minutes and 48.5 seconds, breaking Yang Pu's 4 minutes and 53 seconds; (5) Ling Peigen of Jinling University in the discus throw with 33.15 meters, breaking Chen Guoxiang's 29.68 meters. Generally speaking, the results are not bad, but Lin Guangxing's 100-meter and 200-meter results are particularly good, adding a lot of color to the meet. Lin Xiu fell 5 or 6 meters behind in the 100-meter race, and the result of 11.1 seconds paled the whole field, but Mr. Rong Qizhao's unofficial timing was 11.4 seconds, which is not too far off. In the 200-meter race, he left Ling Yuanyang more than ten meters behind. Moreover, the 200-meter race is not on a straight track, but requires turning a corner. The rain and the loose track made the result even better. If he can practice hard and take Liu Changchun's place, it is within reach. The rain reduced the appeal of the field events. Although Ling Peigen's discus throw of 33.15 meters did not fully realize his potential, it is already a rare result in East China.

Individual Champions 165

First Place: Ling Yuanyang of Jinling University, 17 points (1st in Long Jump, 1st in Low Hurdles, 1st in Triple Jump, 2nd in 200 meters)

Second Place: Xia Xianxuan of Shanghai University, 11 points (1st in 400 meters, 2nd in 800 meters, 2nd in 1500 meters)

Third Place: Lin Guangxing of Shanghai University, 10 points (1st in 100 meters, 2nd in 200 meters)

Third Place: Meng Guangshun of Jinling University, 10 points (1st in 800 meters, 1st in 1500 meters)

Third Place: Ling Peigen of Jinling University, 10 points (1st in Discus, 1st in Shot Put)

Fourth Place: Wang Kaiyuan of Shanghai University, 9 points (1st in Pole Vault, 3rd in Low Hurdles, 3rd in High Hurdles)

Fifth Place: Chen Jiayou of Soochow University, 7 points (1st in High Hurdles, 2nd in 100 meters)

Award Ceremony in the Rain 166

丨Mrs. Tang Liu presents prizes

丨This newspaper awards Lin Guangxing a special prize

At around 5 o'clock, after all the events were over, just as the award ceremony was about to begin, a heavy rain suddenly came. Therefore, the prizes were quickly moved into the girls' dormitory. However, their reception room was hosting visiting advisory groups, so they had to give the awards in front of the dormitory entrance. After Mr. Peng Sanmei, the Director of Physical Education at Shanghai University, reported, Tang Liu, the Director of the Diplomatic Affairs Office in Shanghai, gave a speech, hoping for more efforts. Liu Zhanen, the President of Shanghai University, said that this spirit in the midst of wind and rain was admirable. Finally, Mrs. Tang Liu presented the awards, which were very generous. This newspaper awarded a banner to Lin Guangxing of Shanghai University, who had the best results. The event then concluded.

Suzhou Women's Baseball Tournament: Jinghai Wins the Championship 167

Yesterday, they defeated the Women's Vocational School 21 to 20

Four schools participated in the Suzhou Women's Baseball Tournament. Initially, Huishan was thought to have more hope, as they practiced more actively and had defeated the Liangjiang teams in Shanghai. Yesterday, the two teams met in the final. The weather was unfavorable, as it was raining in Shanghai. The battle with no retreat was quite exciting. Competition Results 168

Those who Practice Football and Basketball 169

"Must-Read Football and Basketball Training Methods" 170

China's Unprecedented Sports Book

Recently, football and basketball competitions have become popular throughout the country, using them to exercise the body and obtain proper entertainment. However, there are many ways to practice football and basketball, and one must follow the principles to easily succeed. Even those who watch the games should understand the game methods to have a strong interest. Mr. Wu Bangwei is a sports expert who has handled competition matters at the China National Amateur Athletic Federation and the Hangzhou National Games. He has a wealth of knowledge and has recently authored three books: "Football Training Method," "Football Rules Q&A," and "Basketball Training Method." "Football Training Method" contains fifteen chapters, including Kicking, Stopping, Following, Dribbling, Tackling, and Hitting; Essential Blocking Methods; Passing and Attacking Methods; Offensive and Defensive Joint Demonstrations; Free Kicks; Goal Kicks; Corner Kicks; Goalkeeping; Carrying the Ball; Penalty Kicks; Player Qualifications and Common Sense; Football Game Training Outline, etc. "Basketball Training Method" has seven chapters, including A Brief Introduction to Basketball Games; Basic Basketball Techniques; Joint Defense Methods; Joint Offense Methods; Special Formation Diagrams; Basketball Team Organization and Management; Basketball Team Training, etc. "Football Rules Q&A" contains one hundred and twenty questions regarding football rules. The content of the above three books is very rich, detailing the training secrets based on scientific methods, with over a hundred illustrations and exquisite printing. They are unprecedented masterpieces in China. Mr. Zhang Boling, the President of the China National Amateur Athletic Federation, highly praised them. All physical education teachers, athletes, and spectators are vying to purchase them. The Football Training Method and Basketball Training Method are each priced at nine jiao (cents), with a special price of eight jiao one fen (cent), and postage of six fen per book, plus five fen for registration. The Football Rules Q&A is priced at four jiao, with a special price of two jiao eight fen. All three books are published by the Qin Fen Book Bureau at No. 39 Xinmin Village, Ma Lang Road, French Concession, Shanghai. The Wenming Bookstore on Nanjing Road, the Shijie Bookstore on Fourth Malu Road, the Nanjing Gonghe Bookstore, the Suzhou Wenyi Bookstore, and the Hangzhou Shijie and Xiaoshuolin bookstores all serve as agents.

Jinan University's School of Education Emphasizes Music Education 176

Educators are increasingly focused on training from early childhood

The School of Education at Jinan University feels that music has a close relationship with education and life. It strongly emphasizes promotion. Yesterday afternoon, taking advantage of the remaining time of the week, a special music conference was held. Principal Xie Xunchu reported on the significance of promoting music education, encouraging the cultivation of the ability to appreciate music, and observing performance results from an educational perspective. Principal Zheng sent Secretary Fan Youshan to deliver a speech, stating that aesthetic education can replace religion and that the school has always promoted music and recreational activities. The performances then began, including mixed Chinese and Western music. In particular, the Shanghai Municipal Council Children's Music Team, led by Miss Wang Ruixian, a musician and music professor at the college, and Miss Dui Xuruo, was highly praised by the audience. All of this originated from the promotion of childhood education by educator Dong Renjian, which shows that educators have focused on music and the need to start training from early childhood. Other wonderful performances included Western music by the Xia Yuehui Society, harmonica ensemble by the China Harmonica Society, English chorus by female students, and the leaf music invented by Lin Maoji.

Also, Jinan University held a school affairs meeting at Yizhixiang yesterday afternoon, discussing the financial allocation for the 20th year in great detail. Principal Zheng was determined not to divert funds allocated to various colleges specifically for academic and cultural research to other uses, in order to emphasize the spirit of promoting culture.

Zhao Zukang Returns to China from the United States 178

Zhao Zukang graduated from Tangshan Jiaotong University in 1922. He served as an engineer in the Qingdao Governor's Office and the Jiangxi Zhaozhang National Highway, Director of the Wuzhou Public Works Bureau, and consulting engineer for the Bengbu Municipal Preparatory Office, achieving remarkable results. In 1929, he was sent to the United States by the Ministry of Railways for further study. He first studied hydraulics at Cornell University, and then went to the Albany Road Bureau to study road materials. Last fall, he represented the Anhui Provincial Government at the New York International Road Conference. This spring, he went to the Washington National Highway Bureau to study road soil science and national road administration. He gained a lot of experience in all of these areas. He departed from Vancouver on the Empress of Asia on the 9th of this month and is expected to arrive in Shanghai today.

Naval Training Aircraft 179

Crashes Again Yesterday, Injuring People 180

Student Li Youzi Dies

The naval training aircraft crashed at the Hongqiao Airport on March 21, killing instructor Chen Changcheng and student Lin Qingyun. It has only been two months since then. Unexpectedly, at 7:30 AM yesterday morning, another unfortunate incident of crashing and injuring people occurred. The person who died on the spot was a naval student:

Mr. Li Youzi 181

The details are as follows. The Ministry of the Navy purchased several light-weight Maes aircraft from England several years ago and has been using them for flight training at the Hongqiao Airport.

At 7 AM Yesterday Morning 182

An instructor from the Aviation Department of the Ministry of the Navy led students in practical training at the airport again. Student Li Youzi

Flew Solo 183

Practiced flying for about half an hour. He was practicing aerobatics at an altitude of about 2,000 feet. The first flip was safe, but when he flipped for the second time, the plane suddenly became uncontrollable. It spun upwards and then plunged straight down. Li Youzi was unable to correct the situation in the plane. The plane fell like an arrow

Crashing at the Airport 184

On the west side of the airport. The wings were shattered and the nose of the plane was buried a foot deep in the ground, which shows how violent the crash was and how

Mr. Li Youzi's Photo 185

Impossible it was for the person in the plane to survive. When the instructors and students in the field saw the plane crash, they rushed to the wreckage to rescue the person. They quickly pulled Li Youzi out. Li was

Gasping for Breath 186

And cried out, "Don't hold me like this, I feel very painful." Who knew that this would be Li's last words. Afterwards, he was unable to speak. The military doctor from the Ministry of the Navy gave him five adrenaline shots in an attempt to save him, but it was ineffective. He passed away

At 8 AM 187

The body was taken to the International Funeral Home on Jiaozhou Road. The body was placed in a coffin at 4 PM yesterday. Chen Shaokuan, Vice Minister of the Ministry of the Navy, went to preside over the ceremony after hearing the news. Shen Dexie of the Aviation Department of the Ministry of the Navy and all the instructors and students went to pay their respects. Li Youzi, also known as Gui Lie, was from Fujian and was 24 years old. He had 60 hours of flying experience. The coffin is temporarily placed in the International Funeral Home. The date of transport back to his hometown has not been set.

Zhang Ji Embarks for Guangdong 188

Wang Chonghui and others personally bid him farewell

Wu Tiecheng sends a letter to Gu Yingfen

Zhang says he will return to Nanjing on the 10th to report

Zhang Ji, a member of the Central Supervisory Committee, was ordered to mediate the Guangdong affairs. He took the French postal ship Sphinx at 11 o'clock yesterday morning to Guangdong. This reporter interviewed Mr. Zhang on board. Zhang, dressed in a gray cloth jacket and black cloth mandarin jacket, was smiling and said that he was confident of achieving peace in the Guangdong affairs. The details are as follows.

Arriving Late 189

At 10:15 AM yesterday, Kong Xiangxi, the Minister of Industry, arrived at the China Merchants Bureau wharf and boarded the ship to bid farewell. However, Zhang Ji himself did not arrive until 10:35 AM. After a brief meeting, Wu Tiecheng arrived, followed by Li Shizeng, Zhang Qun, and Wang Chonghui at 10:45 AM. The ship was about to set sail at that time, and the two sides only stood and spoke to each other from a distance, wishing him a safe journey.

Accompanying Secretary 190

The secretaries accompanying Zhang on this trip to Guangdong are Mr. Sheng Cheng and Mr. Huang Jianfen. Although Wu Tiecheng did not travel with them, he had a personal letter to Gu Yingfen, asking him to take the overall situation into consideration and maintain peace. When Wu boarded the ship to bid farewell yesterday morning, he personally handed the letter to Zhang, which was drafted only yesterday morning.

Zhang's Remarks 191

Zhang told this reporter on the ship yesterday that he was ordered to go to Guangdong to mediate the Guangdong affairs and that he was confident that a peaceful resolution could be achieved. He may have to stay in Hong Kong for a while, depending on the situation. He expects to return to Nanjing to report in ten days. When asked if Chen Jitang had sent a telegram welcoming him to Guangdong, he replied that Chen had not sent a telegram recently, but Gu Xiangqin (Yingfen) had sent a telegram welcoming him.

Kong Xiangxi's Remarks 192

The reporter then had a brief conversation with Kong Xiangxi, who said that the Guangdong affairs were caused by the impeachment telegram from the four supervisory committee members, including Deng Zeru. Now, Mr. Zhang is also a member of the Central Supervisory Committee and was ordered to go to Guangdong to handle this matter, which is most appropriate. In the event of a dispute, the final decision can be made according to the law. There is no reason to use force. What's more, between family members and brothers, the Guangdong affairs are the same. As for the military men of Chen Jitang's generation, obedience is their duty. Once the four supervisory committee members' matter is resolved, there should be no problem.

Steps for the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to Recover Concessions 193

The first step is to send personnel to investigate

Regarding the issue of recovering concessions, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs organized three committees last year to design the plan in groups. It also sent Zhang Wenhua, Deputy Chairman of the Treaty Committee of the Ministry, together with Li Jinglun, Deputy Minister of Political Affairs, Wang Jiazhen, Deputy Minister of Permanent Affairs, Chen Yilin, Counselor, and Ying Shangde, Director of the General Affairs Department, to formulate specific recovery measures. It is heard that this measure has now been decided. The first step is to send personnel to various places to investigate the origin of all concessions, administrative measures, economic conditions, etc., with a deadline of four months. After the investigation and report, the second step will be carried out. The personnel for this project have been planned and will be divided into three zones for investigation: (1) The Yellow River Basin and Northeast regions will be responsible by Huang Yuding, assisted by Inspector Cui Shijie; (2) The Yangtze River Basin will be responsible by Guo Taizhen, assisted by Inspector Zhou Zechun; (3) The Pearl River Basin will be responsible by Tao Shumu, assisted by Inspector Tao Lilian. It is also heard that this order will be issued by the Ministry.

The French Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association Telegraphs for the Recovery of the French Court 194

And Sends a Letter to the French Consul General

To be forwarded to the government of that country

Telegram to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs 195

To His Excellency Minister Wang of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the National Government of Nanjing: Regarding the reorganization of the Shanghai French Court, since Your Ministry raised the issue with the French ambassador, the other party should respect our country's legal rights and return it promptly to honor the relationship between the two countries. However, the French side has always adopted a slow and delayed attitude as a coping strategy. This prolonged delay not only hinders the integrity of our country's legal rights but is also enough to leave a stain on the history of diplomacy. In order to strive to remove the shackles of inequality and complete the unification of the Shanghai Special District Court, the citizens of the French Concession, in addition to sending a message to the French Consul General in Shanghai to forward to the French ambassador to return it unconditionally, hereby telegraph Your Ministry to negotiate the acceptance immediately to comfort the people's aspirations. We respectfully telegraph this to Your Excellency and respectfully ask for your review. The Shanghai French Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association, Chairman Cheng Zhusun, Shang Mujang, et al., bow with utmost anxiety. Respectfully printed.

Letter to the French Consul General 196

Dear Sir: The integrity of legal rights is valued by any country and its people. The legal rights of our Republic of China have been undermined for decades. All the people consider it a great humiliation and vow to redress it. Since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, the people's concept of national sovereignty has become increasingly rich. They have been working to remove the shackles that have violated modern international justice and fairness for the past 80 years. Friendly countries understand the principle of not doing to others what you would not want them to do to you, and provide friendly assistance in the spirit of mutual help and cooperation. This enthusiasm is deeply felt by both the government and the people. Just like the Public Concession adjacent to this concession, its Mixed Court has long been returned to our government and a court has been established according to law. This further shows that the governments and people of the Public Concession have a deep understanding of the way of commerce and diplomacy. However, although the Mixed Court in this concession has been automatically reorganized, it has not fully complied with the provisions of our country's court organization law, and the appointment of moderators and judges is not from our government. This hindrance to our country's legal rights cannot be concealed. China and France have always had a strong relationship. Leaving this stain will inevitably tarnish the jade. The different methods between the two concessions will further cause misunderstandings and increase obstacles to friendly commerce. Based on the spirit of cooperation in the past and with boundless enthusiasm, we hereby convey this special letter, hoping that Your Consul General will forward it to the diplomatic authorities of your government to return the Mixed Court to our government as soon as possible and establish a court in accordance with the law. This will strengthen the relationship between China and France, and the countries related to the Shanghai Public Concession will not be able to excel in the past, and it is also the beginning of a world of great harmony. We respectfully request that you investigate and handle this matter. To His Excellency Mr. Ge, the Consul General of France in Shanghai (May 23, 20th year)

Wang Chonghui's Trip to Europe 197

Expected to depart within a week

Decided to travel via the Chinese Eastern Railway

Wang Chonghui, the President of the Judicial Yuan, has been recuperating in Shanghai recently, declining to see guests. He personally went to the port yesterday morning to bid farewell to Zhang Ji, who was heading to Guangdong. Wang was wearing a dark green silk cotton robe and looked haggard. He told this reporter that his health had recently recovered and that he had decided to depart for Europe within a week to take up his post as a judge at the International Court of Justice in The Hague. He has been packing his luggage in recent days and is very busy. He plans to take a train to Liaoning from Beijing, then travel via the Chinese Eastern Railway and Siberia to Europe. His passport has been processed by the Foreign Affairs Commissioner in Harbin. After arriving in Beijing, he intends to stay for a while to say goodbye to friends and deal with personal matters. The International Court was originally scheduled to convene in August, but due to the dispute over the new customs agreement between Germany and Austria, it is necessary to convene the court early. Therefore, he must rush to attend the meeting.

Zhang Qun's Remarks After Returning to Shanghai 198

The Central Government hopes for a peaceful resolution of the Guangdong situation

He is extremely firm in his opposition to the slaughter tax issue

Building wharves to develop the city center

Mayor Zhang Qun went to Beijing on business on the 18th of this month and returned to Shanghai yesterday morning. After arriving in Shanghai, he visited the Central Committee members who remained in Shanghai, including Cai Yuanpei, Li Shizeng, Zhang Renjie, Wu Zhihui, and Kong Xiangxi, to discuss the mediation plan for the Guangdong situation. At 11 o'clock, he accompanied the committee members to the wharf to see off Zhang Ji, who was heading to Guangdong. A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency interviewed him at his residence yesterday and asked him about various issues. He answered in detail, and the following is a record of his remarks.

The Guangdong Situation 199

According to Mayor Zhang, the central government consistently hopes for a peaceful resolution to the Guangdong situation. The unified image that the National Government possesses today was not easily achieved. Therefore, everyone now, mindful of the difficulties in building it, will take extra care to protect it, hoping for a more solid foundation day by day. Moreover, the communist bandits in Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi provinces have not yet been completely eradicated, and the people of those three provinces are in dire straits awaiting relief. Thus, the central government is currently striving to eliminate the bandit scourge and vigorously planning construction, absolutely unwilling to initiate any disputes that would hinder the aforementioned plans for suppressing bandits and construction. As for the Guangdong situation, it is merely a slight misunderstanding. Once explained in the future, there should be no problems. In short, the people are tired of turmoil, and the majority do not want to disrupt peace.

Slaughter Tax Issue 200

When the reporter inquired about the solution to the business suspension of local butchers due to the slaughter tax issue, the response was that he had expressed his views on the slaughter tax issue some days ago. The current disturbance was entirely stirred up by a few contractors, and the butchers themselves had not had an increased burden placed on them, but were merely being incited by others. Moreover, the slaughter tax is a kind of statutory tax rule, and we only know how to abide by the law, with no other issues. Therefore, he is extremely resolute on the slaughter tax issue.

Pier Issue 201

Also discussed was the recent approval by the Ministry of Interior for the construction of a pier in the Hongkou District Number Two Map area of this city. This was originally part of the plan to construct a central urban area. Three piers will be built east of the central urban area in the future to meet the needs of developing the central urban area. The trunk road for reaching the pier under construction is already under construction. However, to complete the plan for a great Shanghai commercial port, the Wusong River will still need to be dredged in the future.

Chen Shaokuan Discusses the Current State of the Navy 202

Yang Shuzhuang Has Several Days Before Returning to Fujian

Chen Shaokuan, Deputy Minister of the Navy and concurrently Director of the Jiangnan Shipyard, arrived in Shanghai the afternoon before yesterday. Yesterday, a reporter from the Kwok Man Agency called on him and asked about the current state of the navy. The conversation obtained was as follows:

Yang's Trip to Hangzhou 203

Chen briefly stated that Minister Yang (Shuzhuang) had gone to Hangzhou for private matters. After he arrived in Shanghai, he had already reported this by telegram. However, due to matters needing to be discussed, Minister Yang was scheduled to return to Shanghai today (yesterday). He heard that he would still need to go to Hangzhou once more, so his return to Fujian was still a few days away. Currently, the Pu'an warship is still waiting for orders at the mouth of the Songjiang River.

Review Not Yet Completed 204

The naval review has already been completed for a large part of the navy. Those not yet reviewed are only the ships under repair. Therefore, there was a previous order for the Hai Chou and other ships in Shanghai to complete repairs within ten days so that they could sail to Beijing for review.

Recruiting One Hundred Students 205

The Naval Department plans to recruit one hundred naval students on the sixteenth of next month. Each province will recommend fifteen students to come to Beijing for the examination. Those admitted in the future will first study at the Minjiang Naval Academy. After the naval academy being built in Xiangshan is completed, they will be transferred there.

Surveying Commercial Port 206

According to Sun Yat-sen’s "The International Development of China," the central government is developing a large eastern commercial port. Currently, the Naval Department has dispatched the Ganlu survey ship to the Qianjiang River estuary near the Yangtze River to actively conduct surveys. It is expected to be completed in about two to three months.

Lin Zhong in Custody 207

Lin Zhong and others were previously arrested and escorted to Beijing. This matter is entirely being handled by the central government. He had recently been in Beijing and had not heard any news. Fujian's finances are indeed very difficult, but this matter is also being handled by the provincial government. All naval expenditures in Fujian are allocated by the central government. After Minister Yang contacted Chairman Chiang and Finance Minister Song in Beijing this time, it is expected that there will be a solution. He was not deeply aware of this. After the conversation, he bid farewell. He heard that Chen had already gone to Beijing on the night train last night.

Ma Hongkui Denies Entering Gansu 208

There is a rumor that Ma Hongkui, the commander of the Fifteenth Route Army, will be appointed as the chairman of the Gansu Provincial Government. Ma happened to be in Shanghai for business. A reporter from the Kwok Man Agency visited him at his residence yesterday. According to Ma, his elder brother Hongbin is currently in charge of provincial affairs in Gansu. Although there is talk outside that the central government will send him to Gansu, it will definitely not become a reality. The Fifteenth Route Army is still stationed in Tai'an and other places in southern Shandong. His trip to Shanghai this time does not have any special mission.

carried out aggression against weak nations and small countries, some were occupied as territories, and others were reduced to foreign dependencies. Anything that can be said to have the slightest benefit for the imperialists themselves and is sufficient to harm our national sovereignty, damage the lives of our people, and weaken our national vitality is carried out wantonly. Labor Union Telegram 211

The National Conference has already been held in the capital. All political, military, and economic matters have largely reached a unified principle. This is an early symbol of China's unification and peace. We are eagerly anticipating its realization. Unexpectedly, in the midst of firecrackers, there suddenly came the news of Chen Jitang of Guangdong raising troops. How astonishing this is! We common people suffered from the imperialists' oppression of China through wars twenty years ago. The Opium War and the Eight-Nation Alliance's invasion of Beijing are all past wounds.

After the founding of the Republic of China, up until last year, it can be said that there was no year without civil war. We common people have suffered enough and committed enough sins. Fortunately, this year there is finally peaceful unification, and the National Conference has also been held in Nanjing. Everything can be resolved. Moreover, Guangdong is the source of the revolution, and the people of Guangdong have suffered particularly much. Then how can they have the extra strength to supply [the army]? Chen should wake up quickly! Lay down the butcher knife and become a Buddha on the spot. The central government is very lenient and will definitely be able to forgive you. Otherwise, if everything is destroyed, it will be terrible. Sincerely, the Shanghai Steamboat Wood Industry Union Preparatory Committee, the Shanghai Preserved Meat Industry Union Preparatory Committee, the Shanghai Shoe Manufacturing Industry Union Preparatory Committee.

Association Declaration 212

Ever since the founding of the Republic of China, we have been internally subjected to the trampling of warlords and externally subjected to the aggression of the great powers. At a time when the red bandits are causing trouble and the great powers are watching intently, Chen not only does not work for the party and country, but instead willingly acts as a traitor who destroys national law and violates party discipline, disregarding the survival of the country and disregarding the suffering of the people. All citizens are indignant and hate this. We now issue the most sincere and loyal declaration, hoping that Chen will immediately repent and thoroughly correct his past mistakes. Tang Zhaoshi Talks About Liu Jiwen's Lack of Funds 213

After Liu Jiwen, the former Jianghai Customs Superintendent, went to Guangdong, it was recently reported that Liu had embezzled two million yuan of public funds during his tenure, and the Ministry of Finance ordered the new superintendent Tang Haian to investigate. Yesterday, a reporter from the Kwok Man Agency went to the office to visit Tang Zhaoshi specifically for this reason. Tang Zhaoshi, the secretary, received him and was asked about the previous matter. He replied that when Superintendent Tang took office, the handover was handled by the secretary Xu Tigang of the previous administration. It has now been completely completed. The account books and files are very clear, and Mr. Xu is still in this office. As for the matter of embezzling funds, it is even more untrue. When the Changguan was not withdrawn fifty li away, there were no such large sums of money stored in the office. Moreover, the superintendent's funds are well known to the customs tax department. Now the Changguan within fifty li has been effectively abolished since June 1. After the abolition, the regular expenses of this office will be reduced from 7,000 yuan to 2,000 yuan per month. The reduction is 2,000 yuan from the fines of the Changguan and 3,000 yuan from the tax department. To this day, this office has not received an official order from the central government to investigate, so this matter is likely a rumor.

Investigation of Foreign Telegram Checks 216

The Three Companies Have Been Resolved

Japanese Telegrams Also Checked

The case of checking the telegrams coming from and going to the three companies, Daito, Great Northern, and Pacific, has been reported previously. It is essential to check foreign telegrams for our country's international promotion. Therefore, the Ministry of Communications decided to send personnel to check them. During the European War, checks were conducted once before but soon withdrew. After the Ministry of Communications assigned inspectors, the Shanghai International Telegraph Office, entrusted the head of the waterline section, Shen Fuhai, accompanied by the director of Daito Inspection, Chen Wende, the director of Great Northern, Pan Chengdong, and the director of the Pacific, Sun Xichen, and various inspectors to negotiate inspection matters with the three companies. The attitude of the three companies was hesitant, but after the staff repeatedly negotiated and explained the reasons for the inspection, the three companies put forward two points: (A) All inspections of telegrams from various countries must be approved by the Universal Telegraph Association and notified to various countries for investigation; (B) All telegram institutions in Shanghai must be checked uniformly, and that they have not received a reply from the Ministry of Communications. The next day, the three directors went to the three companies and negotiated in person. At that time, the reply from the Ministry of Communications also arrived, and the misunderstanding was cleared up. They took various inspectors to the three companies on the 20th of this month to start work. They are currently engaged in arranging everything, and as soon as the procedures are complete, they will implement the inspection in accordance with the six inspection rules published in the three companies' reports. It is also heard that the Ministry of Communications has also appointed Yu Zezhao, a technician of the Ministry and a member of the International Telecommunications Committee, as the director of the inspection of Japanese telegrams. It is also said that inspectors will be selected to handle various radios in the same way.

Sunday Today, Held Yesterday First

The Great American Evening News said that tomorrow (the 24th) is British Empire Day, the birthday of Queen Victoria. Because it falls on a Sunday, the flag-raising ceremony will be changed to today (the 23rd). At 7:45 a.m., boy and girl scouts gathered at the plaza of the British Consulate General. Sand and Gravel Industry Dispute Changes 218

There are fears that there may be another work stoppage

The sand and gravel industry in this city, after resuming operations in unison the day before yesterday, encountered disputes over the issue of detaining ships and extorting donations yesterday. The various situations are recorded again as follows:

About to Stop Work Again 219

Yesterday, sand and gravel businesses became extremely indignant because the Dachang contractor, responsible for tax collection, employed personnel and dispatched nine police officers to collect sand and gravel taxes in various places along the shore, with respect to sand ships coming to Shanghai. They are planning to suspend operations again to show their resistance.

Sand Ships Respond The Sand Ship Industry sent a letter to the Association yesterday saying: “Regarding the illegal collection of sand management fees and sand prices under various guises in Zhejiang Province, all shipowners are opposed. After reading the newspapers repeatedly, your association has spoken righteously and sought the interests of our shipowners. We are very grateful. We hereby record the documents submitted to the Executive Yuan, the Supervisory Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Zhejiang Provincial Government on the 19th of this month as follows: We hereby present a petition that Zhejiang Construction Hall is setting up improper names and illegally collecting the money. Please immediately cancel the fees so that the government may respond appropriately and alleviate the people’s poverty. The shipowners have been living in the coastal mountains for generations, with more than two to three thousand people relying on the transportation of sand and gravel for a living. In the past, loading and unloading were free, and sales were free, without any levies. Two years ago, treacherous merchants proposed to contract for sand and gravel donations, but the government rejected it because it involved onerous details. The shipowners were grateful for the government's kindness and felt that there would never be any sand and gravel donations again. Unexpectedly, on May 1 of this year, Zhejiang Construction Hall offices and inspection stations were suddenly set up everywhere in Shanghai, Wusong, Dinghai, and other places to issue sand mining permits, regardless of whether it was sand or mud from the outer sea or inland rivers, and a management fee of 50 cents per ton and a sand price of 20 cents were collected. At the same time, Dachang Yitai Company was organized to forcibly buy and sell, otherwise people would be detained and ships would be impounded, and harassment was ubiquitous. Not only was there monopolistic hoarding, but also profiteering. This kind of taxation of goods is actually a disguised likin. At a time when likin is being vigorously abolished, they dare to set up improper names and illegally collect a disguised sand and gravel donation that was not found in the likin era. It is really shocking. The livelihoods of thousands of shipowners are at stake, and the public is in a state of panic. For this reason, we collectively request that you, the leaders, consider the livelihoods of the small people and immediately issue an order to cancel the management fees, sand prices, and other items, and impeach those who disregard political orders in accordance with the law. In addition to the separate submission, we sincerely submit this." Signed by Huang Yuankang, Wu Shengui, Ping Qingfa, Dong Yuesheng, Ping Axiu and others, shipowners of outer sea fishing boats, who have nominated Mr. Zhou Dezheng to come forward and request you to receive him. We are overwhelmed with gratitude."

Builders Meeting 220

Yesterday, the construction industry convened a general meeting of all members in the afternoon to discuss assistance measures due to the sand and gravel industry stoppage. Lu Xiaozuo, a representative of the sand and gravel branch, and more than 30 members of the association attended. Zhang Xiaoliang chaired the meeting and resolved the assistance measures: (1) Present a petition to the Ministry of Finance to urgently request the Zhejiang Provincial Construction Hall to cancel the fees quickly. (2) Request that the municipal party and government agencies immediately stop the collection.

Citywide Butchers to Slaughter First 221

The Chamber of Commerce is Responsible for Resolving the Slaughter Tax

Fresh Meat Available in the Chinese Quarter Tomorrow

The fresh meat merchants in this city have suspended business due to the slaughter tax issue, which has affected the business of restaurants and other businesses, especially the pig industry. Butchers in the concessions, accepting the advice of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, have already slaughtered. Butchers in the Chinese Quarter will start slaughtering today and wait for a solution. The various situations yesterday are recorded separately as follows:

Pig Merchants Request 222

He Laiqing, Zhu Jiugao, Zhang Weisheng, Zhang Fuchen, Sun Kexuan and other representatives of the pig merchants from Jiangbei in Shanghai, totaling 1,326 people, sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday saying: “We, the undersigned, make a living by selling pigs. We transport goods from the production areas in Jiangbei to Shanghai to seek meager profits. More shipments mean more meager profits, and fewer shipments mean more losses. The sales of pigs depend entirely on meat merchants, so the fresh meat industry is our only customer. Recently, the meat merchants in Shanghai have been resisting the high tax issue and appealing to the chamber, hoping to find a solution and stabilize their business. When the news came, our thousands of pig merchants were overjoyed, and according to reports, the Fresh Pig Association has also sent a letter to your chamber, requesting a quick resolution to relieve the meat industry from its difficulties. However, there has been a delay until now without any results, which has caused all the meat merchants in the city to suspend operations, and the greatest impact is on our pig merchants. The source of goods has lost its sales channels, and our livelihoods are becoming increasingly precarious. We are wandering aimlessly and stuck in a dilemma. Moreover, fresh pigs are live goods, and the longer the delay, the more crowded they become in the cargo hold, becoming thinner day by day, and the losses are increasing. If a solution is not found in time, the capital on which we rely for our livelihood will be lost. Thinking about it is frightening, and speaking of it is painful. Therefore, on behalf of our thousands of pig merchants, we call on your chamber to be impartial and resolute and find a quick and effective solution to save the merchants from the water and fire. We are extremely hopeful.” The Municipal Chamber of Commerce replied immediately, “We have received your letter requesting a quick resolution of the meat merchants' suspension due to the slaughter tax issue. The Municipal Finance Bureau has sent a letter requesting that we summon the meat industry representatives to persuade them to resume business first and be responsible for finding a solution. We are now actively working on it and hope to find a reasonable solution in the shortest possible time. This is a reply for your information."

Successive Shipments 223

More than 1,400 shops and stores of fresh meat merchants in the concessions, such as Lujiangjian, complied with the order to enter the market to purchase goods yesterday and reopened for business. Renyuan Slaughter in Jiaxing Road, Juxing Slaughter in Yuezhou Road, Suxi Slaughter in Dawang Temple, Suning Slaughter, Fanggongdong Bureau Slaughter in Nanyang Bridge, and Yinggongbuju Slaughter in Huasheng Road were all slaughtered last night, and fresh meat is available in the concessions today. Meat shops in the Chinese Quarter will purchase goods today and resume business, and fresh meat will be available tomorrow.

Chamber of Commerce Mediation 224

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce, recognizing that the suspension of business by fresh meat merchants has been prolonged and is ultimately not a good solution, has been actively working to persuade them since receiving the letter from the Finance Bureau requesting that it find a way to persuade them. The Chamber invited representatives of the industry to persuade them the day before yesterday, and the meat merchants in the concessions immediately reopened for business. At 2 p.m. yesterday, they invited representatives of the industry again. Representatives Rong Qianchu and Wang Jinwen attended, along with Chairman Wang Xiaolai, Executive Committee Member Wang Yansong, and Secretary-General Zheng Chengqing. They ordered the representatives to persuade all the meat merchants in the city to resume business first and be responsible for working out a solution with the municipal government. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce will guarantee all the slaughter tax amount, and the tax will be paid when the solution is reached. The representatives left feeling satisfied.

Letter to the Finance Bureau 225

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Municipal Finance Bureau saying, "Regarding the collection of slaughter tax on a per-animal basis for the fresh meat industry, business has been suspended for many days. Our Chamber has tried our best to persuade them to resume business first and discuss a solution with the competent authorities. The industry has complied with our advice and will slaughter tomorrow. During the period when our Chamber continues to discuss the solution with your Bureau, please continue to count the number of pigs slaughtered and pay the tax when a solution is reached. Our Chamber is responsible for guaranteeing the amount. Please instruct your Bureau not to detain the pigs so that a smooth solution can be reached. We sincerely hope for your cooperation."

Citywide Slaughtering 226

After accepting the advice of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Fresh Meat Industry Association sent more than a dozen people, including Jin Gui, Mao Bin, Xu Zhiren, and Zhu Zhigao, last night to persuade the various industries in Wusong, Jiangwan, Zhenru, Yinhangdong, Caojiadu, Beixinjing, Xinlaolonghua, Gaoqiao Yinxiang, Zhabei, Xujiahui, Lan Nidu, Lujiabang, Yangjiadu, Dongjiadu, Bailianjing, Yangsi Township, Hunan, Tangjiawan, and other places: (1) All of them will enter the market to purchase goods on the 24th. (2) They will reopen and resume business on the 25th. (3) The slaughter tax will be counted temporarily, and they will wait for a solution.

Wang Yansong Talks 227

A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency visited Wang Yansong, the Executive Committee Member of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, yesterday because the Municipal Chamber of Commerce had taken over the mediation of this case, and asked about the mediation situation. According to Wang, at the beginning of the dispute, the industry association sent representatives to Beijing several times to request him to forward their pleas to the central government to sympathize with the merchants' difficulties and find ways to safeguard them. At that time, he was attending the National Congress and had little time, and the case was a local issue and there was no need to report to the central government. He could wait until he returned to Shanghai to resolve it. While in Beijing, he heard rumors that a few people were manipulating the situation, but after returning to Shanghai, he realized that this was not the case. The meat merchants have expressed that they can accept the small collection of points per animal, but they are requesting a reduction in the tax rate because they cannot afford it, which is not too much to ask. He recently decided that the meat merchants' prolonged suspension of business has caused considerable losses, so he strongly urged the meat merchants to resume business first, and he will be responsible for working out a solution with the mayor. The meat merchants have recently accepted his advice and will reopen for business tomorrow.

Tax Exemption Approved for the Transportation and Sale of Homespun Cloth 228

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce sent a letter yesterday to the Yarn and Cloth Dealers Association and the Homespun Cloth Industry Association, stating: "Regarding your previous letter requesting that we forward to the Ministry of Finance a request for tax-exempt transportation permits for homespun cloth being transported and sold to Hong Kong and the Northeast Provinces, we have forwarded the request via telegram and repeatedly urged approval. On the 22nd of this month, we received a response from the Ministry of Finance, document number 12799, which stated: 'We have received your telegram. The General Taxation Bureau has submitted a case stating that homespun cloth, woven by hand by farmers using small amounts of cotton yarn already subject to the consolidated tax as raw material, and transported and sold abroad or to domestic areas not subject to the consolidated tax, should be granted exemption from customs export duties in order to maintain the livelihoods of the poor. This has been approved and the Customs Administration has been instructed to notify all customs tax authorities to act accordingly. You are hereby notified.' We are sending this letter for your information and compliance." Respectfully addressed to the Shanghai Yarn and Cloth Dealers Association and the Homespun Cloth Industry Association.

Local News

Grand Opening Ceremony of the National YWCA Association 231

A Precursor to the Success of the National Women's Movement

Madame Huang Zuoting's Labor Deserves Commemoration

The new building of the National YWCA Association has been under construction since last winter, and the main beams and pillars have been completed. On the afternoon of the 22nd of this month, at 4 p.m., the association held a foundation stone laying ceremony, and Madame Huang Zuoting was invited to lay the foundation stone. Here is a record of the grand occasion:

Around 4 p.m. on the 22nd, Chinese and foreign guests arrived one after another. At that time, more than a dozen people including the committee members of the Association, Madame Mei Huaquan, Madame Xia Jinlin, Dr. Su Shouzhen, Ms. Jin Mao Yunqin, and the General Secretary of the Association, Ms. Ding Shujing, stood respectfully at the entrance of the venue to receive the guests cordially and seat them one by one. It is estimated that there were about 300 people attending the ceremony to offer their congratulations, including representatives from the China Vocational Education Society, the local municipal government, various agencies, the Cosmopolitan Student Association, and major Christian organizations in Shanghai. It was a grand occasion. In addition to the usual ceremonies such as paying the highest respect to the Party and National Flag and the portrait of Dr. Sun Yat-sen and respectfully reading his will, the chairman, Madame Zheng Zhangcheng, reported on the preparation process of the new building and the origin of the site. Then, Madame Mei Huaquan, chairman of the building committee, gave a detailed account of the history of the new building. Finally, Madame Huang Zuoting performed the foundation stone laying ceremony. At that time, workers slowly raised the foundation stone to the designated position with a lifting machine and placed it properly. Then, Madame Huang personally took a few spoonfuls of plaster with a silver hoe and lightly touched the joints of the foundation stone as a symbol of personally sealing it. The foundation stone was placed under a large window sill on the left corner of the new building, about the height of a person. The window faces the street and is sure to be seen by passersby. The foundation stone is engraved with eight large Northern Wei characters, "Walk to Know Truth, Truth Releases Steps," which is the motto of the Association. The handwriting is clear and the style is strong, making it an excellent work of art. Madame Huang, who presided over the foundation stone laying ceremony, has a deep relationship with the YWCA movement in China. Madame Huang has been serving in the YWCA for more than 20 years, and has made admirable contributions to the Association's affairs, both large and small. It can be said that she has earned the honor of performing this grand ceremony as a reward for her hard work. As for the silver hoe used during the foundation laying, the chairman respectfully presented it to Madame Huang as a permanent souvenir. After the ceremony, important figures from the municipal government, Ms. Lin Kecong, Ge Baohang, executive member of the Drug Resistance Association, and Mr. Zhong Ketuo, Mr. Zhu Lide, general secretary of the Christian Association, and Zhang Jun, chairman of the Youth Association, delivered speeches, earnestly expressing their views and encouraging the audience. The audience was moved. The gist of the speeches was that the YWCA's foundation laying ceremony today is not only to congratulate the committee members and staff of the YWCA from the perspective of a tangible foundation, from which a solid foundation will be built and the future is limitless. The laying of this foundation stone actually contains an intangible aspect, which is even more worthy of celebration, that is, this foundation laying is tantamount to laying a solid foundation for the future of the Chinese women's movement, and showing that the success of our future women's movement is as stable as Mount Tai. (2) This foundation laying is a sign that the YWCA movement in China has reached the right track. (3) Looking at the women's groups in China today, the only one with organization, system and national scope is the YWCA. Therefore, the laying of this foundation stone should be solemnly congratulated and encouraged by the people of the country. Now that the foundation has been laid, the Association has added another responsibility to guide women across the country. In short, although the ceremony itself was to lay a small foundation stone, it seemed insignificant, but the atmosphere at the venue at that time and the expressions in the speeches of the guests were full of infinite solemnity and infinite joy. Finally, the students of the Chinese and Western Girls' School sang and dispersed, and went to the second floor of the new building to enjoy tea and snacks. At about 6 o'clock, the hosts and guests dispersed happily.

Jing'an Temple 232

Today's Buddha Bathing Ceremony 233

If the Weather is Good

It Will Be More Prosperous Than in Previous Years

The Jing'an Temple in Western Shanghai always holds a Buddha bathing ceremony on the eighth day of the fourth month of the lunar calendar. This year, the Public Works Department issued a notice restricting the setting up of stalls. After the abbot of the temple, Zhifa, repeatedly negotiated with the Public Works Department, the order was revoked. The stalls along the way are like combs, and when the lights are turned on, it is like entering a city that never sleeps. Local gentry have donated money to hire musicians, and various agencies and schools have assigned security guards and boy scouts to serve in the temple to celebrate together. Its grandeur is unprecedented. It is expected that if the weather is good today, the bustling situation will be more prosperous than in previous years.

Shaanxi Disaster Film 234

The Plight of the Victims Brings Tears to One's Eyes

Generously Donate to the Emergency Relief Association

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau responded to the request of the Shaanxi Disaster Emergency Relief Association and sent the Shaanxi film to major cinemas for screening, as reported in the previous newspaper. Yesterday morning, the film was premiered at the Carlton Theatre. Although it was raining continuously, there were still many enthusiastic viewers. Some women in the audience were brought to tears by the plight of the victims, showing that this situation is truly beyond the imagination of the people who live in comfort in Shanghai. It is said that the film will still be screened at the Carlton Theatre at 10 a.m. next Saturday, with an additional feature film. From the 31st, it will be screened at the Central, Shanghai, and Odeon theatres. Those who feel compassion for the displaced victims and generously donate can send their donations directly to the Shaanxi Disaster Emergency Relief Association on Yunnan Road, the General Office of the Red Cross Society on Second Avenue, or to the temporary donation boxes at the entrances of the Central, Shanghai, and Odeon theaters, so that they can gather sand into a tower and lift the victims from their misery, which is a supreme virtue.

American Soldiers Push People into the River 235

Two American Soldiers Fight Each Other by the River

A Chinese Worker Tries to Mediate and Suffers a Calamity

Still Not Found by Evening

Yesterday afternoon, around 2 p.m., two sailors from an American warship docked at the Xin Kai He Riverfront hired two rickshaws and got off in front of Jinyuan No. 8 Warehouse. The two then started fighting each other near the No. 11 pier, as if they were drunk. As they fought, they gradually moved towards the pier, as if they were about to fall into the river. A coolie who was watching rushed to Limalu and reported to Chinese Constable No. 165. The constable arrived at the riverbank and saw the two sailors fighting on the pier, seemingly about to fall into the water. He went forward to try to persuade them, but was pushed away. He retreated and stood on the shore. At that time, one of the sailors was half-submerged in the water. Seeing the danger, the coolie resolutely went down to the pier to save him. Unexpectedly, the other sailor pushed the coolie into the river, and he immediately disappeared. Seeing the disaster, the constable took the two sailors to the No. 16 Wharf Police Station, reported the situation, and a patrolman from Jinyuan Wharf No. 8 testified. The police station detained the two sailors and sent detectives to investigate the scene and dock workers to search for the coolie. Because it was high tide at the time, he had not been found by 4 p.m. Only a pair of broken shoes and a hat were found.

Grave Robbery 236

Three Corpses Reburied Last Month

Shen Zhongping Offers Reward to Catch a Thief

Grave robbery cases in Pudong and Western Shanghai are often heard of. The Yao family's ancient tomb on Avenue Paul Doumer in the French Concession was robbed by thieves again last night, and the bones were scattered. The details are as follows:

History of the Yao Family Tomb 237

The Yao family's ancient tomb is located at the northwest corner of Avenue Paul Doumer and Rue Alfred W P in the French Concession, behind the German School, in the 27th Bao 5th Tu of Shangyi County. The Yao family is the maternal family of the late Shen, the owner of the Yongxiangfeng Funeral Supplies Store on Sanmalu, and a famous wealthy merchant in Shanghai. The coffin of Shen's maternal grandfather was made of nanmu wood, extremely strong, and contained a lot of gold, silver, and jade. He died decades ago. The Yao family's ancestral tomb was originally near Jing'an Temple, but the three coffins were moved to the 5th Tu of Avenue Paul Doumer due to the construction of roads by the Public Works Department. Every Qingming Festival, Shen's descendants would go to sweep the tomb.

Details of the Robbery 238

The night before yesterday (the 21st), around midnight, three thieves carrying grave-robbing equipment dug up the three coffins and split them open with axes. They stole the ancient jade and gold objects from the coffins. The corpses had already rotted, leaving only bones. The thieves had three wooden boxes, and they put the bones in the boxes and reburied them, intending to cover up their tracks. While they were working, dawn broke. Neighbor A got up and went to the field to pick vegetables and saw the situation. He ran to the Yongxiangfeng store on Sanmalu and reported to the young master of the store, Shen Zhongping. Shen drove to the scene by car, but the thieves had already fled. Only the three coffins were split open, and the bones were scattered all over the ground, a very tragic sight.

Reporting to the Police and Offering a Reward 239

Shen immediately reported to the Lujiiawan Police Station, which sent detectives to investigate and confirmed the facts. They are now tracking down the coffin thieves, and Shen has also published a reward notice and is preparing three sets of high-quality coffins to rebury the bones.

Pirates Enter the Wusong Estuary 240

Two Merchant Ships Robbed Outside the Estuary

Pirates Escort Ships to Wusong to Collect Money

Water Police Arrests One Pirate After Receiving Report

Around 5 p.m. on the 18th of this month, a Wang Fuji official salt ship was sailing through the Red Boat waters outside the Wusong Estuary when two pirate ships suddenly came after it, firing shots as a warning. They surrounded and robbed the ship from both sides. The shipowner, Wang Shanzai, was taken to the pirate ship. Around 6 p.m., an ice-fresh ship sailed to the same waters and was also intercepted and robbed by pirate ships. Both ships were then taken by the pirate ships to Xiaosha and anchored. On the next day, the pirates took the ice-fresh ship out to sea. Gong Yuesheng was tied up on the official salt ship, and two pirates were sent to monitor the ship, ordering it to sail towards Wusong. Yesterday afternoon, around 3 p.m., the official salt ship sailed into the Wusong Estuary. The pirates ordered the ship to dock near the Hei Futong (Black Buoy) near Paotai Bay. One pirate remained on the ship to monitor it, while the other escorted Gong Yuesheng from the ice-fresh ship to shore at the Paotai Bay Foreign Wharf, took a train to Shanghai to collect money to redeem the ship. Around 4 p.m., the helmsman of the official salt ship, Yang Azeng, took advantage of the pirate's inattention and sneaked to the stern of the ship, escaped ashore in a small boat, and ran to the 16th Team of the 4th District of the Wusong Water Police to report the crime. Captain Wu Zhishan of the team immediately sent police to be stationed at the station, secretly waiting for the pirate to go to Shanghai. At the same time, he sent Inspector Jiang of the 3rd Team to lead a large number of water police to take a small steamer, silently, to the Hei Futong official salt ship. At this time, the pirate had become aware and attempted to jump into the water and escape, but it was too late and he was arrested and taken back to the team headquarters. The pirate confessed his name as Wang Shaochuan, 42 years old, from Haimen, Zhejiang, a boatman. He used to work on Panxinglai's ship and was kidnapped by pirates in the Da Ji waters some time ago. He was forced to act as a pilot on the pirate ship. The day before yesterday, the pirates ordered him to guard the salt ship with another pirate who was at large and to sail to Wusong. Because it was raining and he was hungry, he wanted to get off the ship after eating, but was arrested by the soldiers. The pirate leader's surname is Wang. There were nine pirates on the pirate ship, with eight rifles and seven pistols. They ordered me to stay on the salt ship and wait for the ice-fresh ship to go to Shanghai to get money and redeem the tickets. I was just urging for money for the pirates. Captain Wu, after verifying the confession, immediately ordered Inspector Jiang to lead the police to take a small steamer to Xiaosha outside the Wusong Estuary to pursue the remaining pirates. The two pirate ships anchored in Xiaosha saw the small steamer from afar and knew that something was wrong. They immediately took advantage of the wind and set sail and fled. Seeing the situation, the small steamer immediately chased after it, but it was already dark and the wind and waves in the waters outside the estuary were very strong. The small steamer was afraid of encountering danger and had to return, so the ice-fresh ship that had been kidnapped was able to take the opportunity to escape and return to the Wusong Estuary, which can be said to be the best of a bad situation. The police, who were secretly waiting at the station, did not see any trace of the pirates until the evening and reported back to the team. Captain Wu considered the case to be serious and sent the arrested pirate to the 4th District for review that night.
