Datong Line at $110 Per Ounce

Since gold has become more expensive than silver, the common people have suffered indirect pain, and the price tags for red gold jewelry in the city's gold shops have exceeded 100 yuan (per ounce). People from all walks of life had hoped that the price of gold would fall, but yesterday the price tags of the gold shops suddenly rose. The Datong Line was exchanging at 110 yuan per ounce, and the Xiaotong Line was also exchanging at 108 yuan. The common people, seeing the continuous increase in the price of gold, were worried.

The Eastern Section of Pucao Road Was Completed Yesterday 244

Pucao Road in Western Shanghai starts from Chengjiaqiao on Hongqiao Road, passes south through Hongqiao Town to Yaojiawan Bridge, and extends east along the Caohejing River to the gate of the Youmin Xiqin Institute in Caojing Town, and ends at Zhongshan Road in Longhua Temple. The entire road is 16 li long. It was originally named Qinglong Road, but the municipal government's funds were unavailable, so it was temporarily postponed. Now, Mr. Huang Jinrong has donated a large sum of money to build the eastern section of the road first to facilitate transportation, starting from Caojing West Town, along the river to the Huang family ancestral hall in Laofenshan. The road surface is entirely paved with stones and has been completed, which is convenient for the villagers who come and go.

The Health Sports Meeting of the YWCA Ended Successfully 245

Yesterday was the last day of the Shanghai YWCA Health Sports Meeting. The weather was not good in the morning, it was raining, but it cleared up at noon, and the number of people attending suddenly increased. The places where physical examinations and vaccinations were given were especially crowded, and the venue was packed. In the afternoon, there was a speech by Dr. Fu Wenshou, who, based on his experience, put forward the following thoughts on the issue of infant care: (1) There are four errors in infant care methods: (1) Mothers lack common sense of infant care, (2) Old ideas are not easy to break and hinder new knowledge, (3) Entrusting infants to ignorant maids, resulting in illness or the development of bad habits, (4) Improper feeding after weaning. It must be known that feeding children only with porridge and rice is not enough to meet the needs of the child's body. Infants must have a small amount of milk, eggs, fruits, vegetables, grains, and meat every day in order to develop a strong body. It is important to prevent the following every day: (3) Delay and panic after illness, (4) Disregard for the advice of doctors, (5) Lack of well-equipped pediatric hospitals, (6) Lack of health care cooperation between medical experts and philanthropists. The above points should be paid attention to by us. Correct the first four examples if you have them, and encourage yourself if you don't. As for the latter two, we hope that all walks of life will advocate and promote them in order to achieve the goal and wipe out the shame of being a sick man. After the speech, the Jingwu Gymnastics Association's national music was followed, and the melodious silk and bamboo added color to the conference. The "Child Labor" skit by the association's labor union group was also quite alarming. In the three days, a total of more than 300 women and children attended the meeting for physical examinations, injections, and vaccinations. This does not include the students of the association and the ladies of the dormitory. There were about 2,600 visitors to the conference, and many ladies from all walks of life took this opportunity to learn about the YWCA and join as members, and many children joined the Children's Health Association established by the association, so that they can be examined once a week to achieve the purpose of health care. It is also heard that the association will regularly select those children who are physically sound from this examination and re-examine them once, and give awards according to the rankings to encourage them. In addition to the awards prepared by the association, there are also gifts from various milk powder companies.

Superintendent of Pacification Sends Detectives to Escort Wanted Criminal, Zhi Jingui 253

Lawyer Zhi Yan Requests Retrial

Trial Postponed Due to Absence of Lawyer

Zhang Zhijiang, Superintendent of Pacification for Jiangsu, previously sent a document to the French Concession court stating that the bandit leader Zhi Jingui, also known as Zhi Xingkui or Zhi Xiaotao, had committed serious crimes in the Jiangbei area and fled to Shanghai, hiding in the French Concession. He requested cooperation in apprehending and extraditing him. The Chinese and Western authorities informed the police, who arrested Zhi and handed him over to the court. After interrogation, the court ruled that Zhi should be extradited to the inland authorities for trial. Zhi, dissatisfied with the verdict, hired lawyer Gu Jirong to file an appeal for a retrial. The appeal was granted, and Zhi was summoned yesterday. First, the prosecutor stated that he had received a letter from Gu Jirong, the plaintiff's representative, stating that he had to leave Shanghai due to important matters and requested a postponement of fourteen days. Subsequently, the lawyer representing the Superintendent of Pacification's office stated that the plaintiff's lawyer's request for postponement was strongly opposed. As Zhi Jingui was a wanted criminal, the Superintendent of Pacification's office attached great importance to the case and had sent dozens of officers and soldiers to Shanghai to escort him. If the trial was postponed, they would suffer irreparable losses. He requested that the trial be opened today and that the court order Zhi Jingui to be handed over to the officers to be taken back for trial as soon as possible, to avoid further losses. After consultation, the Chinese and Western judges ordered a postponement of the trial for seven days.

Danyang Kidnapping Victim Still Not Found 254

Two More Bandits Arrested, One Handed Over to the Public Security Bureau

Two children from the Wang and Li families in Danyang County were kidnapped by bandits in February. Aside from one bandit captured by local authorities, three male and female suspects were arrested by the Municipal Public Security Bureau in conjunction with the police the day before yesterday and sent to the Special District Local Court. The court ordered that Li Wenxiang be handed over to the Public Security Bureau for further investigation, while Liu Dehuai and Li Wei were detained for further verification, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. After being handed over to the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Li immediately underwent a preliminary hearing. He confessed that Li Sihong and Ding Shangzhen (also known as Ding San), two Jiangbei natives residing at 126 Tongzhou Road, were also accomplices. Investigator Qin Bin was dispatched to the Harbin police station to cooperate with the Chinese and Western detectives in secretly arresting Li and Ding at the address. Subsequently, according to Sihong's confession, the kidnapped Wang and Li children were hidden in a house at 576 Zhoushan Road. However, when the detectives rushed to investigate, they found that the bandit gang had already fled with the children. Yesterday morning, police officer Li Ding brought investigator Qin Bin to the Special Court to request extradition. After questioning by Judge Luo, Li Sihong was handed over to the officer to be taken back to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for further investigation. It remains to be investigated whether Ding Shangzhen was indeed one of the kidnappers in the case, and evidence still needs to be collected. He was ordered to be temporarily detained at the police station, awaiting a joint trial with Liu Dehuai and Li Wei on the 29th of this month.

Suzhou Woman Sues General Manager of Jiangnan Bank 255

General Manager Qian Zengbao Absent Due to Illness

Court Orders Defendant to Appear

Yao Shunhua, a 29-year-old woman from Suzhou, had an informal relationship with Qian Zengbao, General Manager of Jiangnan Bank. They initially resided at No. 29, Lane Fai, Rue Lafayette in the French Concession, cohabiting for one year and seven months. Since September of last year, Qian has stopped visiting Yao. Unable to support herself, Yao hired a lawyer to sue Qian for violating Article 244 of the Criminal Code, accusing him of using deception to make a woman believe they had a marital relationship and submitting to his fornication, as well as Article 310, abandoning a person without the ability to support themselves whom he was legally or contractually obligated to assist, support, or protect. She also filed a private suit, demanding that the defendant pay her 60,000 yuan in lifelong alimony. The court issued a warrant for the arrest of Jin Wanrong to Bai Tongli, 598 Rue Beclague, notifying the defendant to appear in court for questioning, as reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Ge Zhitan of the Second Criminal Division summoned the defendant. Qian Zengbao was absent, and lawyer Jiang Yiping appeared in court on his behalf. Yao Shunhua stated that she had cohabited with the defendant since November of the seventeenth year of the Republic. Qian initially told her that he had no wife at home. Half a year into the cohabitation, she discovered that he already had a legal wife. As things had already progressed, she had no choice. In September of last year, Qian suddenly claimed that her behavior was improper and wanted her to commit suicide. He even gave her opium to take. She swallowed the opium but was later saved. Since then, Qian has not visited her. Unable to support herself, she moved from No. 29, Lane Lafayette, to No. 366, Juqing Lane, Xin Zha Road. She requested that the court rule according to the law. Lawyer Jiang Yiping then stated that the defendant was absent today because he was ill. The plaintiff's lawyer immediately stated that since the defendant had been legally summoned but claimed illness as the reason for his absence, he should provide evidence of his illness. Lawyer Jiang replied that even if the plaintiff's lawyer did not mention the legal summons, he would still have to state that Qian Zengbao did not reside on Rue Beclague but at No. 152, Route du Père Froc in the French Concession. Rue Beclague was the home of his relatives. Furthermore, all the articles of law cited by the plaintiff were inapplicable because she was still young and had not reached the point of being unable to support herself, and she could not prove that she was Qian's wife. According to her, there was no matchmaker, no exchange of birth charts, and, furthermore, the plaintiff was a prostitute. If a prostitute were to sue a customer for abandonment, everyone would feel threatened. This trend should not be encouraged, and the plaintiff's suit should be dismissed. Judge Ge Zhitan, believing that the defendant's presence was necessary, ordered a postponement of the trial to the afternoon of May 30th.

Hu Hongyuan Convicted on Two Counts 256

Counterfeit Cigarettes and Illegally Made Seal

Combined Sentence of Seven Months and a Fine of 300 Yuan

The Shanghai Tobacco Consolidated Tax Inspection Office of the Ministry of Finance previously discovered that Hu Hongyuan was evading national taxes. Inspectors were dispatched to No. 721, Qipu Road, where they seized several boxes of tax-evading cigarettes, some of which were counterfeit products of the Delon Tobacco Company. Hu was arrested and brought before the Special District Local Court, accused of tax evasion and counterfeiting, as reported in this newspaper. It has now been learned that during the search, a counterfeit seal of the cigarette tax bureau with the words "Examined and Approved" was also found. The police added a charge of illegally making a seal. The tax evasion portion of the case was recently tried by a judge in the Summary Division of the Special Court. The evidence was conclusive. If the case were handled according to the Stamp Tax Regulations, he would have been subject to extremely severe penalties. However, the judge, considering that he was a small businessman who was unaware of the consequences and was a first-time offender, granted leniency and reduced the penalty to twice the amount of tax evaded, ordering him to pay a fine of 112 yuan as a light punishment. As for the counterfeiting and illegally making a seal charges, both were local cases. Judge Luo of the Local Division of the Special Court held a joint trial yesterday morning. After the police lawyer Zhang Tianyin and the Delon Company's representative lawyer Wu Linkun presented the details of the case, Judge Luo questioned the defendant Hu Hongyuan. Finding the evidence in both cases to be sufficient, he immediately pronounced the verdict: three months imprisonment and a fine of 300 yuan for counterfeiting, and six months imprisonment for illegally making a seal, with the sentences to be served consecutively for a total of seven months. The fine was 300 yuan. The counterfeit cigarette seals were confiscated.

Joint Inauguration Ceremony of Executive Committee Members of All County Districts Held 260

Held at the County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee Yesterday

The Executive and Supervisory Committee members of all districts of Shanghai County held a joint inauguration ceremony yesterday (23rd) at 10:00 AM in the auditorium of the County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee. The Executive and Supervisory Committee members from each district who attended included Zhang Yi, Weng Zhuoying, and Jin Lemin from the First District; Xu Pengcheng, Li Youtian, and Ding Borong from the Second District; Ding Hanzhang, Sun Jiafeng, and Ma Xiwen from the Third District; Zhang Jingye, Qu Wenbo, Liu Jianhong, Wang Chengyao, Lu Huisheng, and He Shoumei from the Fourth District; Ding Guanyan, Huo Guiliang, Xue Qirong, Zhou Yuanliang, Sun Tao, Jin Yongxin, Kang Qiang and others, a total of twenty-eight people. The County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee members Lü Zhe, Tao Yishan, and Jiang Yanchou were present. Jiang Yanchou served as the oath administrator, Deng Huanian as the master of ceremonies, and Chen Guoan as the recording secretary. After the formalities, (1) the oath takers raised their right hands and read the oath. (2) The oath administrator Jiang Yanchou delivered a speech, briefly stating: (1) He hoped that everyone would be the Party's "running dogs," abide by the oath, and be loyal to the Party. (2) He hoped that everyone would act as "salt," as salt can prevent corruption. The current society is ugly and becoming increasingly corrupt. He hoped that everyone could act like salt to combat corruption. (3) Zhang Yi, the representative of the oath takers, delivered a reply. (4) Tao Yishan of the County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee delivered a speech, briefly stating: (1) Establish a revolutionary worldview. (2) Supervise the activities of the district branches. (3) Absolutely obey the orders of higher authorities. Finally, a group photo was taken, and the meeting adjourned. It was already twelve o'clock.

Health Bureau Administers Inoculations Yesterday 261

Preventing Cholera

In order to reduce cholera cases this year, the Municipal Health Bureau has been actively sending doctors and nurses to various organizations, schools, and factories in the city to administer vaccinations. From May 1st to May 22nd, a total of 50,214 vaccinations were administered. The bureau dispatched sixteen doctors and nurses yesterday to encourage vaccinations in major factories in Nanshi, Zhabei, and Wusong. The time was set from 1:00 PM to 12:00 AM.

Labor Dispute at Jinxin Cloth Factory 262

The Jinxin Cloth Factory, located on Nancang Street, Lujiabang Road, Nanshi, dismissed six workers, including Huang Cai, Gou Jiang Hegen, Chen Afa, Huang Pinzhou, and Yao Zushun, without cause on the 5th of this month. The Shanghai South District Cotton Weaving Industry Union sent representatives to negotiate with the factory, but to no avail. The union petitioned the Party and government agencies for assistance. The Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau instructed the factory to allow the six dismissed workers to return to work immediately. However, the factory adopted a strong stance and refused to reinstate them. All fifty-odd workers at the factory sent representatives to negotiate with the factory yesterday, but without results. All the workers then unanimously went on strike and petitioned higher authorities to mediate as soon as possible to prevent the labor dispute from escalating.

Property Owners Association Announces Establishment of Conciliation Committee 263

The Shanghai Property Owners Association sent a letter to its members and related organizations yesterday, stating: "We, the Association, have observed that rental disputes have been occurring frequently recently. The historical morality of peaceful coexistence between landlords and tenants has been destroyed. Minor disputes lead to animosity, and major disputes lead to lawsuits, causing losses to both parties. The state has now established a mediation process in addition to litigation for civil matters, hoping to restore our country's inherent virtue of peaceful coexistence. Landlord-tenant relationships are civil matters and should be based on kinship. How can they be treated as enemies and engaged in litigation? If reasonable and fair conciliation is carried out, can major disputes not be turned into minor disputes, and minor disputes into no disputes? Based on this principle, a Conciliation Committee has been established. Kui Yanfang, Dou Yaoting, Jiang Bingsheng, Yao Shantao, Liu Hongyuan, Yuan Ludeng, and Zhang Xingcun were elected as committee members to handle disputes between landlords and tenants through conciliation. We are sending this letter for your information and instructions."

Appeal for Disaster Relief in Ningxia 264

The Chinese Red Cross Society recently received a telegram from the Ningxia Provincial Party Headquarters stating: "Our province has long been occupied by the Feng Faction warlords, who have levied heavy taxes, a hundred times more than in the past. They have squeezed the people dry, leaving them unable to survive. When the Feng army collapsed, bandits ran rampant, and people were displaced. Hailstorms, rats, and locusts have caused repeated disasters. The granaries are empty, and food is running out. The extremely poor are starving to death, and the middle class is becoming displaced. Gathering to rob grain and committing suicide by family have become common occurrences. The current disaster situation cannot be fully described, and the future is uncertain. As there are no farming tools in the homes and no grain for seeds, the spring planting will not happen, and the autumn harvest is uncertain. If urgent action is not taken to provide extensive relief, the people of the province will perish. The hidden dangers in the Northwest are unimaginable. We have just arrived in this land and are deeply shocked by what we see. We respectfully present the local disaster situation for your consideration. We respectfully request that you quickly report to the National Government and allocate large sums of money for emergency relief to save the remaining people. The National Government has approved the allocation of 20,000 yuan from the Gansu relief funds, but this is a drop in the bucket and has little effect. Without allocating additional large sums of money, this extraordinary disaster cannot be averted. We implore you to consider the disaster-stricken people and advocate for relief, and we hope that you will generously provide grain to support this righteous cause. We are kneeling and begging on behalf of the millions of starving people in the province. The telegram is urgent. Please give it your attention. Chinese Kuomintang Ningxia Provincial Party Affairs Special Commissioners Fang Deren and Zhang Tianwu."

Effective Tomorrow

Various shipping companies operating between Shanghai, Chongming, and Haimen have been affected by the increase in coal prices and have decided to change the passenger fare from small dollars to big dollars starting tomorrow (25th) to compensate. Chinese Bus Workers Request Double Pay on Race Days 267

Company Has Not Yet Responded

The Daily News reports that the workers of the Zhabei Chinese Public Bus Company recently requested double pay on race days due to the high cost of goods and the difficulty of making a living. This is because more people take the bus to the racetrack on race days, resulting in higher revenue. However, the company has not responded because it has suffered significant losses this year, and the workers' compensation is already relatively good.

Customs Allows Transportation of Gold Jewelry 268

Requires Certificate from Chamber of Commerce Stating Not for Export

Tang Haian, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, and Mei Weiliang, Customs Commissioner, issued a joint notice yesterday stating: "Notice regarding the joint issuance of a notice: Upon receiving an order from the Ministry of Finance stating that all refined gold and gold jewelry transported to treaty ports, if the local Chamber of Commerce provides a certificate to the Customs guaranteeing that they are not for export, should be allowed to be transported, we should comply. All merchants are hereby notified."

Social Affairs Bureau Continues to Mediate Binding Industry Dispute Yesterday 269

The Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau continued to mediate the dispute over the revision of treatment conditions in the binding industry yesterday morning. Representatives from the labor union, including Xu Fuli, Chen Zhaoqing, and Ren Changfu, and representatives from the trade association, including Ding Handong, Lou Weiqing, and Xu Hanqing, were present. Wang Bing presided over the meeting, and Wang Zhiqin recorded the minutes. After a lengthy discussion, the two sides strongly disagreed on the second item, the apprenticeship issue. The chairman announced that it would be temporarily shelved. The third item, that the employers should not dismiss workers or union officials without cause and that workers must be given one month's notice of dismissal, and the union must be notified at the same time, was passed. However, this does not apply to temporary workers whose employment is less than three months. The same applies to workers who do not wish to work. When hiring workers, preference should be given to unemployed members of the union. However, these unemployed members must be approved by the government as qualified to enjoy this right. The fourth item, working hours, stipulates nine hours per day. Night shift work is five hours for one shift and three hours for half a shift. Sundays are eight hours for one shift. During working hours, workers must not leave the workplace without permission. After the two items were discussed, the meeting was adjourned due to time constraints. It was decided to convene a conciliation committee again at 9:00 AM on the 26th to continue mediation. The Public Security Bureau and the Municipal Party Headquarters were also invited to send representatives to attend.

Robbery on Zhonghua Road Yesterday 270

The home of Sun Bingsheng, located at No. 10, Huashun Lane, Zhonghua Road, Nanshi, was robbed by five bandits at around 1:00 AM yesterday. Two of the bandits were wearing black robes, and the other three were wearing blue cloth short shirts and trousers. They all spoke with local accents. Two of the bandits were armed with pistols. They robbed Sun of a gold bracelet, four gold rings, a pair of gold bracelets, a platinum watch, and other items. After the robbery, they left with the stolen goods. Sun reported the incident to the Second Sub-precinct of the Second District and requested that they investigate and apprehend the robbers.

Truck Fire 271

Yesterday morning at 12:15 AM, a cargo truck, number 1334, caught fire suddenly at the entrance of Yuanfang Lane, Yuanfang Road, Hongkou. The Hongkou Fire Department dispatched a vehicle to the scene and extinguished the fire. The truck was completely destroyed.

Hongxing Hosiery Factory Price Reduction Announcement 272

Hongxing Hosiery Factory, located at the entrance of Manting Lane on Wuma Road, is known for its "Dog Head" brand products, which are sold worldwide. The brand is known for high quality and low prices and has gained a good reputation over time. Recently, due to the summer season, the factory is holding a major price reduction for 21 days starting on the 10th of this month. At the same time, a free bar of soap will be given away for three days. The store is extremely busy, and despite the continuous rain in recent days, the number of customers has not decreased. Among the items sold, long silk stockings for men and women at one yuan for two pairs, silk dancing socks at one yuan for two pairs, and long cotton socks for men and women at one yuan for five pairs have been the best sellers. In addition, dozens of dozens of undershirts, shorts, straw hats, and felt hats are sold every day.

Public Security Bureau Seeks Claimants for Two Male Corpses 273

Yesterday, the Municipal Public Security Bureau received a report from the Fifth District stating that on May 17th, a male corpse was discovered north of the Weishi Leather Factory on Xitiyu Road. The name of the deceased is unknown. The male corpse is estimated to be in his twenties, wearing a gray tweed jacket and pants, blue shoes, and white socks, with a flat-top hairstyle. The cause of death appears to be being crushed by a steam vehicle. In addition, according to a report from the Second Precinct of the Fifth District, on May 16th, a male corpse was discovered behind the Beihui Guild Hall on Zhongxing Road. The name of the deceased is unknown. The male corpse is estimated to be in his forties and appears to be a beggar who died from illness. Relatives of the deceased are requested to come forward to claim the bodies.

The Utilization of Laborers' Leisure Time 274

Social Bureau Publishes Book

The Municipal Social Bureau has previously published a series of books, including "Statistical Methods for Labor Disputes," etc. Recently, to meet social needs, it has published a book entitled "The Utilization of Laborers' Leisure Time." This book was compiled by Mr. Mo Ruoqiang of the Bureau, who selected materials from reports from various countries obtained by the International Labour Office and further referenced the actual situation in this city. The content is novel and the text is concise. Anyone concerned about labor issues should read this book. It is said that the printing is now complete and will be sold at the China Bookstore and the Commercial Press in this city. The actual price is only 30 cents per copy.

Public Concession Police Department Seeks Information 276

The Public Concession Police Department is seeking information. On March 27th of this year, at approximately 8:45 AM, Chinese Constable No. 2124, while riding in a private car at the intersection of Fuxu Road and Chengdu Road, pursued two armed Chinese men. The two men were riding in rickshaws and fled along Fuxu Road and Notre Dame Road in the French Concession. During the pursuit, one of the men fired a gun at the Chinese Constable, causing serious injury and death. Anyone with information about the private car in which the Constable was riding and its driver is requested to personally notify the Deputy Inspector of the Criminal Division of the Police Department at 18 Hankou Road (telephone numbers 60743 and 19474) or the nearest police station. May 23rd.

Weather Report 284

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the Yangtze River Basin and the coastal areas here are cloudy with rain or fog due to the passage of a low-pressure system moving northeast-eastward. The cyclone in this area and the East China Sea is strengthening. There is rain and northeast wind on the coast of Shandong. There is still no weather report from Taiwan. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 66.4 degrees and the lowest was 58.8 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 74.5 degrees and the lowest was 56.7 degrees.

Free Talk

World Snippets 285

— Hai Ke

The British White Star Line's regular mail ship "Olympic" made its maiden voyage in 1929. The ship is equipped with unusually thorough facilities, including artificial sunlight, tea dances, and a cinema showing the latest films.

In England, between 1915 and 1926, early marriages were often discovered. Three were under the age of fourteen, thirty were under the age of fifteen, and two hundred and ninety-two were under the age of sixteen. Their legally stipulated marriage age is fourteen for men and twelve for women.

American automobile magnate Henry Ford is the world's richest man. He is 67 years old this year. He enjoys walking, running, logging, and dancing as daily exercise to strengthen his body.

The most valuable cat in England is the Abyssinian breed. There are fewer than thirty in the whole country. Therefore, most cat owners regard them as treasures.

The highway in Ontario, Canada, is called "The King's Highway". The road signs are shaped like shields and marked with a crown. Each road is marked with a number.

There are currently 300 female dentists in England. When the British Dental Association was founded 50 years ago, there was not even one.

Record of Graceful Humor 286

— Gui Zecheng

The other day, Pan Zhiquan hosted a banquet for Xun Huisheng and Yan Jupeng at his villa on Maiyang Road. More than ten people were present, including Wu Jing, Xiong, E Lügong, and Lin Lao Zhuo, Yang Cheche, etc. They exchanged toasts, and the scene was very grand. Everyone present knew that Mrs. Pan was good at singing and encouraged her to try. Mr. Pan suddenly said, "If you really want her to try singing, please allow me to leave for a while." Everyone was surprised by his words. Mr. Pan continued, "It's nothing. As soon as I hear her sing, I feel goosebumps all over my body and can't stand it for a moment. If you must ask her to embarrass herself, I can't refuse, but I must leave for a while." Then everyone burst into laughter and stopped the discussion of singing at the banquet. Since the proposal to sing a song was made, everyone asked Huisheng to sing first. After being asked again and again, she sang two excerpts from the hairpin phoenix and the Lantern Festival riddle. Her voice was round and her words were correct, like pearls rolling on a jade plate. Everyone present applauded. Huisheng is very modest and has the best interpersonal skills. This time, when she came south, she was accompanied by Mr. Shu Sheyu to visit literary giants whom she had never met before. On the evening before going on stage, she specially visited Mr. Cao Mengyu. Mr. Cao has always had a connection with bearded actors. This time, with the introduction of Sheyu, he also agreed to support the performance. In addition, there is a social butterfly in Zhenjiang named Cha Peicang, who is good at singing Qingyi and resembles Yu Shuang, and has been praised by many people. Recently, she changed her plan and wanted to learn from the strengths of various schools and meet the Four Great Vajras. At that time, she happened to be in Shanghai. Hearing that Huisheng was coming, she wanted to see her. Before leaving, she asked Cao, "I have met three of the Four Great Vajras. I have never met Huisheng. Can you introduce me to her? Please write a letter to me. I will come to Shanghai again." From this, we can see the magic power of Huisheng. She is indeed a deep person.

Three Poems of Lake Tower 287

— Xiao Die

My father built a house on the lake, titled "Rest and Recuperate," facing Yu Huang in the distance and next to Su Xiao nearby. The bright windows, twenty-four in total, face the lake, and the scenery is beautiful in rain, moon, wind, and sunshine. My father has already written several lyrics, and Cui Mei is ashamed to respond with poems. I am not literary, so I will write a short poem to record the scenery at that time.

The heavy clouds have not yet closed the surrounding mountains. Poplar catkins and flowers fly all over the ground. The empty courtyard is quiet with no one. Red roses dance wildly on half the wall. A thousand points of oars are rushing in the lake. Waves far suppress Su Gong's embankment. The night in Hangzhou in April is dark. Overcoats are often deceived by the east wind. The season is sometimes cold and sometimes warm. Like a clear or misty mist, it is subtle. The spring breeze can bloom for a few days. Many branches are already sparse on the ground. I urge you to cherish flowers in time. Don't wait for the rain to turn into empty branches. (Lake Tower Rain Arrives)

Woke up to the sound of birdsong. The first sun is in the forest table. The green mountain is bathing for me. We both smile at each other. Open the window and look at the lake. The mirror surface is shining. Who is going to Nanping? Call the boat out early. Gradually far away from the blue sky. The little point at the end of the eye is small. (Sunny day)

The guests in the building left and the moon had not yet risen. Tourists gradually returned as the sun set in the west. Leaning on the railing for a while, all sounds are empty. Reading a book and not sleeping, sitting alone at night. Sparse stars flickering, the lights are there or not. Distant buildings see the lights. The moon gradually brightens towards midnight. I feel that there are people talking in the lake. The water is close at hand, the sky is upside down. Three or five small boats come and go. Not a ghost, not an immortal, can't be picked up. A long flute floats with the mountain rain. (Sitting at night watching the moon)

Unprecedented Rat Disaster 288

— Wen Ruoweng

Jiao Yitang, a member of the Central Committee and a member of the Legislative Yuan, recently returned from an inspection of Party affairs in Shaanxi. On the 18th, he reported on the strange disaster in Shaanxi at the memorial week of the Legislative Yuan. He said that the tragedy and strangeness of the Shaanxi disaster were unprecedented. Anyone who set foot in Shaanxi, even if blind and deaf, could know the strange tragedy of the disaster. There are 400,000 unburied starved corpses. The stench reached thousands of miles. You can know it by touching your nose. Now the whole of Shaanxi has reached a situation where there is a road but no one walks on it. The former motor road is now full of Artemisia and thorny paths. All you can see is piles of white bones. I don’t know where the cars have gone. As for the reasons for the construction of the Shaanxi disaster, one is locusts, the second is drought, and the third is an unprecedented rat disaster. In an area of ​​Shaanxi, thousands of five-colored rats suddenly appeared within a day. They were everywhere. The big ones were like civets, and the small ones were like ordinary rats. Cats and dogs were startled and avoided them. The mottled colors filled the mountains and fields, to the point that people could not set foot. Within the next day, all crops were lost. After another night, the warehouses were empty. By the morning, the people's food was exhausted and the rats were gone. Those Chinese and Westerners who went to study could not understand where they came from. The villagers said that they were transformed from white insects in cow and sheep dung, but this has not been proven. However, it must not be viviparous. (Viviparity cannot reproduce so quickly.) That can be asserted. As a result, thousands of miles of empty storage. The people were starving. It became an unprecedented strange disaster. Thousands of people died of hunger without coming back. I really don’t know where such a rat disaster came from. However, there are no people left in Shaanxi. When Mr. Jiao spoke, he pointed to the various colors on the wall case as proof, saying that the colors of rat hair are all available and not as simple as those of ordinary rats. Alas. The coming of the catastrophe is so peculiar. It is really unprecedented. What are the scientists going to study from and prevent it from happening again, or to prevent it. That is also the gospel of mankind.

British Girl's Strange Way of Distinguishing Tea Leaves 289

— Huang Yingdai

Ever since Chinese tea leaves were introduced to various European and Western countries, some Westerners have actually stopped drinking coffee and started drinking tea. Therefore, the sales of tea are also developing day by day. When we walk through major cities in various countries, we can see tea shops everywhere. There is a tea shop in England. The owner of the shop is a young girl named Miss Margaret lrving. When she purchases various tea leaves, she always tries them to identify the taste of the tea. However, because she tries every day, the price of tea she spends is as much as 5,000 pounds a year.

Her method of identifying tea is indeed unique. She can indeed be called the King of Tea Identification. The value of the tea leaves imported into her store every year is more than one million in gold coins. Her business is indeed not small. It is said that after her trial, not to mention being able to identify whether the tea is fresh or not, she can even identify the place of origin. This may be an exaggeration. However, the quality of the tea, after her identification, can indeed not be hidden from her.

Speaking of her method of identifying tea, it is also very interesting. There are many small teapots and teacups prepared in her home. When purchasing, she puts each kind of sample in a small teapot in the same amount. She pours boiling water down. After six minutes, she pours it into a cup and tries it one by one. According to her, the method of identifying tea leaves is that the color is light bronze, and the quality is the best. This is originally her experience, and we cannot help but believe it.

Record of the Health Model of the First People's Education Center in Songjiang 290

— Yi Gong

On the fifteenth day of the month, the Jiangsu Provincial Education Museum held a health exhibition in Songjiang. More than 40 counties came. More than ten rooms were on display. There were statistical tables, or propaganda pictures, or wax models. All of them were familiar to us. Among them, there was a special tree banner with a unique design, and it was the health model made by the staff of the First People's Education Center in Songjiang that was scrambled for by the audience.

There are a total of twenty models. Each model is about a foot in size and is rectangular in shape. The hygienic matters are made in the middle, with both positive and negative aspects. There are people dumping garbage, people setting up watermelon stalls, people sweeping the floor, people dusting, people brushing their teeth, people sticking dirty teeth, people urinating along the way, people collecting riverbanks to wash rice and wash toilets, people playing ball in the playground, people collecting tea gardens and sipping tea, there are people lying on a couch, swallowing clouds and puffing out fog, there are people drunk, turning tables and overturning chairs, there are people tying their chests in front of the mirror, there are people giving birth, there are people who have not gotten up at the third watch, there are people swatting flies, there are people removing mosquito larvae, there are people taking a bath, there are people vomiting, there are people sitting on bamboo beds, digging their feet and smelling their fingers, there are people giving vaccinations, there are people drinking water from a smoking ground, there are people drinking well water, there are people having a meal together, there are people carrying coffins, all of them are vividly portrayed and lifelike. In total, there are eighty-four men, women, old and young. The walking ones, the sitting ones, the standing ones, the sleepers, the hunched ones, the crawling ones, the bare-chested ones, the weeping ones, the ones in Western clothes, the ones in Chinese clothes, all of them are fully prepared. Except for the two sleepers and the three dead people, the rest all have work to do. All of them are full of expressions. The gestures are about to come alive. There are thirty-two houses, eight beds in total. There are iron beds, wooden beds, bamboo beds, and half beds. There are eighteen tables, twenty stools in total. There are both Chinese and Western round ones. There are four lamps in total. There are two electric lamps, one Western lamp, and one opium lamp. There are fifty-eight bowls, twenty-six pots, three clocks, and forty-two bottles. There are twenty-five windows and six boxes. Three are foreign fire, and three are cigarette boxes. There are two plates, one for meals and one for cigarettes. There are screens, wardrobes and mirrors. All of them are arranged in an orderly manner, just like real ones. There are countless characters, such as the posters on the walls of tea shops, and the screens on both walls of the study. They are all written in regular, cursive, official, and seal characters. Even the toilets and garbage bins have small fly heads. And add phonetic symbols next to them. Not to be hasty in small things. Others such as mosquitoes and flies, mosquito larvae, etc. Utensils such as chopsticks, spoons, needles, etc. are all available. The decoration is appropriate, and the view is magnificent. And its raw materials are nothing more than cardboard and colors. In summary, its value is less than a few gold coins. And it can attract people so much. It can be said that it gathers the elite of art and exhausts the power of propaganda.

News from the Art World The famous painter Mr. Feng Chaoran has more than 20 female disciples. Mrs. Pan Gongzhan, the director of the Social Bureau, is also one of them. Now, Ms. Sun Qionghua and Zhang Yanhua, the two ladies who received the earliest education, initiated a collection of paintings from Songshan Cottage at Yiguanxuan on May 24.

Round the Yellow Sea (12) 291

— Huang Yanpei

Arrived in Tokyo on the 6th.

I haven't been to Tokyo for more than ten years. I have heard a lot about the reconstruction after the great earthquake. The city streets and houses are more decent than before. So, with great hope, I paid attention to observing. Cleanliness is an inherent beauty of Japan. As far as the city appearance is concerned, it is indeed great and magnificent, and it is very different from before. The transportation facilities are especially surprising. In addition to the ground railway, there are also elevated railways and underground railways. But there are not many passengers. The streets are not crowded. Not to mention other places, even the busiest Ginza doesn't feel lively at all. Especially the restaurants everywhere, business is very slow. Everyone is talking about the recession. recession

In China, I don't take a car unless it is necessary. When I arrived in Japan, I took a car a lot. Not to show off, the price is really too cheap. In Tokyo, any street has cars that solicit business at any time. The sign says, "One yen in the city" means that within this city, no matter how far the road is, the price is only one yen per ride. In fact, it only costs fifty cents. The so-called one yuan is still a facade.

From Maguan to Tokyo, the stations are extremely dense. There is probably a station every ten minutes. The platforms at each station are extremely long. Even small stations are much longer than the Shanghai station on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway in our country. But the people at each station that passed were not many, and even fewer goods were seen. When asked why, they all said it was a recession. recession.

Rotary Club

Hawthorne's Turning Point Case (23) 292

— Cheng Xiaoqing

He suddenly made a gnashing sound and said, "Hey. This is damn killer, it made me suffer so bad. If I see him, I will risk my life and beat him half to death." Hawthorne replied with a smile, "Half dead is too heavy. Discount it in half. That will be enough. —Now take a look. Do you know the man in the suit?" Qiu Kui looked carefully in the direction that Hawthorne pointed. He shook his head suddenly and replied, "I don't know him. Could this person be—" Hawthorne stopped him and said, "Okay. Wait a minute and talk about it." I thought to myself that this person was clearly the evil young man. How could Qiu Kui say he didn't know him? Could it be that he was really an accomplice, deliberately trying to avoid it?

At this time, the waiter brought the dishes one after another. While I was eating, I secretly watched the man and woman across the corner. So no matter whether it was smoked fish or fried meat, I couldn't really tell what it tasted like when it was sent to my mouth. I quietly asked Hawthorne, "What are we going to do now? If we let him go again today, I will be really angry." Hawthorne replied in a low voice, "What do you plan to do?" I said, "I really can't care about legal issues now. I'm prepared to vent my anger first. I'm willing to be subject to criminal sanctions if I hurt him." Hawthorne smiled again, "Where has your sanity gone? Is this action worth it? Please rest assured. Since he used the turning method to fool us, we can also copy it and follow suit. You can be patient for a while. I know that Hawthorne's method of dealing with the same turning method must be to use Qiu Kui. However, Qiu Kui has already denied knowing this person. How can our plan be implemented? Just at this moment, I saw Hawthorne's eyes flash and he quickly took out his wallet from his pocket, ready to pay the bill. His expression suddenly became tense. I looked back and immediately found out the origin of the tension. It turned out that the young man and woman at the corner table had both gotten up and stood up. The man first put a black velvet cloak on the woman. Then a waiter also put a coat on the man. The coat was exactly gray Qing tweed. There were also square stripes. A copper pot hat was also dark brown. It was exactly the same as what I saw that night. The two people put on their clothes. The woman was in front and the man followed behind. Then they went out through the glass door.

Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat market in the morning, the prices of various months were higher by 3-4 fen due to the cloudy and rainy weather and the good quotes for foreign wheat. However, after the weather cleared, the bulls sold off, and the prices fell by 2-3 fen. When the market opened in the afternoon, it was increasingly difficult to set the price for foreign wheat due to the sharp rise in the gold price. The general inland gangs, due to the weather, were actively buying in, causing the quotes for each month to rise again. In the end, the current upward trend started due to the bad weather, and recently it has been driven by the gold market. The so-called "when it rains, the house leaks", and there are still many disturbances ahead. As a result, the current month rose by 5 fen compared to the previous day, June rose by 6 fen, July rose by 4 fen, August rose by 5 fen, September rose by 4 fen, and October rose by 3 fen.

The Sugar Market Central Sugar Opens 5,000 Bags 321

The various 划盘 prices rose uniformly

Yesterday, the sugar market's production area telegrams showed that the Cuban current sugar price had not changed. The New York sugar futures price for September was 22, December was 1.30, each falling by 1 fen compared to the previous telegram. The price for March next year was 1.37, falling by 2 fen. The current and futures prices of Java sugar remained unchanged. In the association market 划盘, due to the rising exchange rate and increasing buying enthusiasm, the prices of outgoing goods rose sharply. The成交價 for荷 sugar No. 24 coarse sand white was 11 taels, 0 qian, 7 fen and a half to 1 qian, Hong Kong goods were 11 taels, and the trading was quite lively. The market situation was extremely good. No. 20 medium sand white was 10 taels and 6 qian and a half, with both entry and exit being sluggish. Japanese sugar rose at the same time, and the sharpness of the trend had the impression of a rapid rise. N was 11 taels, 1 qian to 1 qian and a half. TK was at the same price. SH was 10 taels and 8 qian. T was 11 taels, 4 qian, 7 fen and a half to 5 qian. YT was 11 taels. YRO was 10 taels and 6 qian. Minghua goods were 10 taels and 6 qian and a half. YP was 11 taels, 0 qian and 4 qian to 4 qian and a half. TM was 10 taels and 9 qian. The prices were all shouted higher in the later market, and the market situation was all good. The factory market had Central Factory opening 5,000 bags of Japanese sugar AEAR due in June and July, with a price of 4 yuan, 4 jiao, and a half for Japanese gold, and the market situation was stable. The 號盘 had domestic Huanggangqing opened several hundred bags yesterday, with a price of 8 taels and 2 qian per yuan. Because the inventory was particularly thin and the output from the production area was not旺, the market price rose but remained attractive.

Northern and Southern Goods, 泉泡圆 Ground Price Rises by Six Yuan 322

Quanzhou large 泉泡桂圆 has recently been rising in the Shanghai market, and the new flower seedlings in the local area are very rare. It is expected that the harvest will be poor, so the ground price suddenly increased by 5-6 yuan. The inventory of goods is also not much. Yesterday, the Xinyuanan Wheel entered from the Quanzhou port, carrying only three hundred boxes, so the sentiment is even more stable.

Silk and Tea Foreign Firms: Silk Market Still Lifeless 323

Yesterday, the local foreign silk market remained lifeless. It was found that overseas silk prices had fallen sharply, and telegrams reported a gloomy situation. Chinese silk merchants, considering the extremely low silk prices and the huge losses incurred, adopted an increasingly passive attitude. Yesterday, only Berthold & Jennings handled eleven bales of Huang Yao silk, and Hsiang Lee handled five bales of coarse Huang silk, with prices continuing to weaken.

Xiaoshan Spring Cocoon Harvest Exceptionally Poor 324

Overall, only about 30% remains... Cocoon prices are high, at sixty yuan.

In various towns and villages in Xiaoshan, such as Kanshan, Toupeng, Shushan, Shanxinan, and Guali, this year's early silkworms suffered purely from adverse weather conditions, and the late silkworms also suffered losses of 60% due to unfavorable climate. New cocoons have already been put on the market, with only a dozen or so cocoon trading houses open. The quality of the cocoons is inferior, and the price of superior cocoons is high. Improved breeds of cocoons were already being sold for sixty yuan yesterday.

Shexian New Tea Shops: Sales Relatively Brisk 325

Sales of tea leaves from Shexian County have always relied heavily on shops and firms. Last year, flower tea from the southeast and northern China sold extremely well. Therefore, shops and firms were very eager to stock up on tea. In addition, this year's new tea was picked early, and the goods were of excellent and tender quality. Those shops and firms searching for supplies were particularly enthusiastic, driving market prices up to hundreds of yuan, a record high. Foreign firms are now wary of the soaring market prices. Furthermore, they observe that the new tea from Sui'an County, which local Shanghai firms are processing into Chun Mee tea, is selling at prices similar to last year. Since the cost is higher than before, but the selling price remains the same, the losses are obvious. Foreign tea firms, faced with this situation, see that the market trend is too strong to reverse or reduce prices, and they can only limit purchases as a temporary strategy.

Piece Goods: Piece Goods Amidst Rapidly Rising Gold Prices 326

Our Factory's Cotton Cloth 327

Yesterday, a surge in prices occurred, with fine cloth being the strongest. The reasons are the low silver prices, the rapid rise in the gold market, and the consequent increase in commodity prices. In addition, a large quantity of fine cloth has already been purchased by Tianjin merchants, and this month's goods are almost exhausted. Therefore, all brands have increased by five cents. Blue Flying Fish is priced at seven taels and nine mace, Trumpet Boy at seven taels and five mace, Colored Ball at seven taels and four mace and five candareens, and Blue Chicken at seven taels and two mace and five candareens. Fine twill has increased by two and a half cents. Sentiment towards coarse cloth has also slightly improved. Eleven-pound Three Rabbits and Three Deer are both priced at five taels and four mace, and thirteen-pound Double Flags at six taels and six mace and five candareens. Jardine Matheson's blue-striped bleached cloth and Golden Pagoda bleached cloth are consistently in short supply, while sales of coarse twill remain sluggish.

Eastern and Western Piece Goods 328

The market situation yesterday was such that, due to the soaring gold prices, all goods rose rapidly. Fine broadcloth was higher by about one cent. Lakeside Pavilion now requires three mace and three candareens and five cash, and Three Friends Picture requires three mace and two candareens and five cash. Bao Qiu (Precious Ball) goods are still out of stock. Straight tribute flannel, Mount Mogan, Hunting Goose, Double Boy, and Deer are consistently out of stock. Tianjin merchants purchased twenty-five pieces of Three Friends Picture at a price of three mace and two candareens. Yue Hua cloth is increasingly expensive, with large patterned cloth priced at two mace and three candareens and five cash, and medium and small patterned cloth priced at two mace and three candareens. The speed of the increase was truly unexpected. Cotton flannel from Changsha merchants saw considerable purchases, with Yang Guifei (Consort Yang) red priced at two mace and three candareens, and Wu Meiren (Black Beauty) in concubine color priced at two mace and two candareens. Yuan Yu silk also rose yesterday, with Bamboo Forest priced at eleven taels and seven mace and five candareens. However, white crepe remains stable, mainly because the remaining stock is still abundant.

Metals and Exchange Market: Raised Prices Also Rise 329

As the exchange market fell frequently in the past few days, the cost of various metal goods increased by one or two cents of cash in an invisible way. Local merchants, aware of this, are holding firm on prices. Therefore, yesterday, the standard of all goods was raised considerably. British tinplate has already risen by one mace and five candareens, selling for sixteen taels and two mace. Pig lead has increased by two mace, selling for fifteen taels and eight mace and five candareens. Over four hundred bars were traded yesterday, purchased by merchant groups from Sichuan and Tianjin. British steel plates, seven and a half cents thick, can also be sold for six taels and seven mace and five candareens. The asking price for eighteen sheets of black iron sheet has risen to twelve taels. It is said that six or seven hundred bundles were sold, mostly to enamel factories. Flat white iron corrugated sheet The market situation was improving yesterday due to hoarding by speculators. New iron wire, new lead wire, and French nails previously had little trade, and the market situation was weak and the standard was weakening. Recently, due to good sentiment, the market price has rebounded, with French nails estimated to sell for nine taels and two mace and five candareens, new lead wire for fourteen taels, and new iron wire for fourteen taels and two mace and five candareens. In addition, the market situation for other iron products is related to sentiment, and all are showing an upward trend.

Coal: Over a Thousand Tons of New Beipiao Coal Dust Arrive 330

Beipiao bituminous coal dust has a large market in the Tianjin area, so its arrival and dispatch here have been rare for a long time. As of yesterday, the Chang'an Shipping Line brought 1,700 tons, which were unloaded at the Beipiao Main Warehouse. However, this batch of goods is only for the company to deliver orders to various factories. Although there is a market price, it is still quite difficult to buy a small amount.

Youth Corner

China Public Photography Research Association 331

— Heart

The Chinese people have never paid much attention to the art of photography, so it is inevitable that we lag behind others in this field. This is a very sad phenomenon. In recent years, it seems that more people are paying attention to it, but their purpose is mostly to photograph beautiful modern girls, taking such pictures to gain economic benefits. Their purpose is not to study the art of photography, but for personal material gain.

The China Public Photography Research Association was organized by Wang Xiangqin, Cao Jiji, Xie Chengbing, Tang Ouzhou, and others. They are all very interested in photography and have a considerable amount of research. The association has been established for more than a year and has already had good results during this time. They exhibit their daily photographic achievements once a week, and have already exhibited more than twenty times. Each exhibition has been praised by students.

Recently, in addition to exhibiting their achievements at the school, they have published their more successful works in publications such as "The Young Companion" and "China Pictorial" in order to provide them for the appreciation of the majority.

Chinese photography is far behind Western photography. I hope that friends who are interested in photography will work hard and not only catch up with Western photography, but also surpass them. As long as we are willing to study hard, progress will be rapid.

Finally, I would like to express my sincere hope that the members of the China Public Photography Research Association will work harder to seek deeper learning. At the same time, I hope that friends at home who are interested in photography will respect art and never disregard everything solely for personal gain.
